                <div id="previewWarnings"></div>
                <div id="previewColumns" style="display: none;"></div>
                <div id="previewInvalidDetails" style="display: none;"></div>
                <div class="info-box" id="previewEmpty">
                    O preview dos dados aparecera aqui apos gerar o preview.
                </div>
                <div class="table-wrapper" id="previewTableWrap" style="display: none;">
                    <table>
                        <thead>
                            <tr id="previewHeader"></tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody id="previewBody"></tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>
            </section>
        </main>
    </div>

    <script>
        const previewButton = document.getElementById('btnPreview');
        const confirmButton = document.getElementById('btnConfirm');
        const clearButton = document.getElementById('btnClear');
        const fileInput = document.getElementById('excelFile');
        const statusLine = document.getElementById('statusLine');
        const previewTableWrap = document.getElementById('previewTableWrap');
        const previewHeader = document.getElementById('previewHeader');
        const previewBody = document.getElementById('previewBody');
        const previewEmpty = document.getElementById('previewEmpty');
        const previewTotal = document.getElementById('previewTotal');
        const previewInvalid = document.getElementById('previewInvalid');
        const previewWarnings = document.getElementById('previewWarnings');
        const previewColumns = document.getElementById('previewColumns');
        const previewInvalidDetails = document.getElementById('previewInvalidDetails');

        let currentToken = null;
        let currentColumns = [];

        function setStatus(message, type) {
            statusLine.textContent = message || '';
            statusLine.className = 'status-line' + (type ? ' ' + type : '');
        }

        function resetPreview() {
            currentToken = null;
            currentColumns = [];
            previewHeader.innerHTML = '';
            previewBody.innerHTML = '';
            previewTableWrap.style.display = 'none';
            previewEmpty.style.display = 'block';
            previewTotal.textContent = '0';
            previewInvalid.textContent = '0';
            previewWarnings.innerHTML = '';
            previewColumns.style.display = 'none';
            previewColumns.innerHTML = '';
            previewInvalidDetails.style.display = 'none';
            previewInvalidDetails.innerHTML = '';
            confirmButton.disabled = true;
        }

        function renderMessages(messages) {
            previewWarnings.innerHTML = '';
            if (!messages || !messages.length) return;

            // Group by severity
            const errors = messages.filter(m => m.severity === 'error');
            const warnings = messages.filter(m => m.severity === 'warning');

            if (errors.length) {
                const box = document.createElement('div');
                box.className = 'alert-box';
                box.style.backgroundColor = '#450a0a';
                box.style.borderColor = '#991b1b';
                box.style.color = '#fca5a5';
                box.innerHTML = '<strong><i class="fas fa-times-circle"></i> ERRO — Importação impossível:</strong>';
                const ul = document.createElement('ul');
                errors.forEach(m => {
                    const li = document.createElement('li');
                    li.textContent = m.text;
                    ul.appendChild(li);
                });
                box.appendChild(ul);
                previewWarnings.appendChild(box);
            }

            if (warnings.length) {
                const box = document.createElement('div');
                box.className = 'alert-box warning';
                box.innerHTML = '<strong><i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i> Avisos:</strong>';
                const ul = document.createElement('ul');
                warnings.forEach(m => {
                    const li = document.createElement('li');
                    li.textContent = m.text;
                    ul.appendChild(li);
                });
                box.appendChild(ul);
                previewWarnings.appendChild(box);
            }
        }

        function renderColumnInfo(detected, missing, unmapped) {
            previewColumns.innerHTML = '';
            if ((!detected || !detected.length) && (!missing || !missing.length)) {
                previewColumns.style.display = 'none';
                return;
            }
            previewColumns.style.display = 'block';
            const box = document.createElement('div');
            box.className = 'alert-box info';
            let html = '<strong><i class="fas fa-columns"></i> Colunas detectadas:</strong><div class="columns-grid">';
            (detected || []).forEach(c => {
                html += `<span class="col-tag mapped">✓ ${c}</span>`;
            });
            (missing || []).forEach(c => {
                html += `<span class="col-tag missing">✗ ${c}</span>`;
            });
            html += '</div>';
            if (unmapped && unmapped.length > 0) {
                html += `<div style="margin-top:6px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b">Colunas extras (nao mapeadas): `;
                html += unmapped.slice(0, 8).map(u => u.source || u.mapped_as).join(', ');
                if (unmapped.length > 8) html += ` ... +${unmapped.length - 8}`;
                html += '</div>';
            }
            box.innerHTML = html;
            previewColumns.appendChild(box);
        }

        function renderInvalidDetails(invalidRows) {
            previewInvalidDetails.innerHTML = '';
            if (!invalidRows || !invalidRows.length) {
                previewInvalidDetails.style.display = 'none';
                return;
            }
            previewInvalidDetails.style.display = 'block';
            const box = document.createElement('div');
            box.className = 'alert-box warning';
            let html = `<strong><i class="fas fa-times-circle"></i> ${invalidRows.length} linha(s) invalida(s):</strong><ul>`;
            invalidRows.slice(0, 5).forEach(ir => {
                const errors = (ir.errors || []).filter(Boolean).join(', ');
                html += `<li>Linha ${ir.row}: ${errors}</li>`;
            });
            if (invalidRows.length > 5) html += `<li>... e mais ${invalidRows.length - 5} linha(s)</li>`;
            html += '</ul>';
            box.innerHTML = html;
            previewInvalidDetails.appendChild(box);
        }

        function renderPreview(columns, items) {
            previewHeader.innerHTML = '';
            previewBody.innerHTML = '';

            columns.forEach(col => {
                const th = document.createElement('th');
                th.textContent = col.sourceColumnName || col.name;
                previewHeader.appendChild(th);
            });

            items.forEach(item => {
                const tr = document.createElement('tr');
                columns.forEach(col => {
                    const td = document.createElement('td');
                    const value = item[col.name];
                    td.textContent = value === null || value === undefined ? '' : value;
                    tr.appendChild(td);
                });
                previewBody.appendChild(tr);
            });

            previewEmpty.style.display = 'none';
            previewTableWrap.style.display = 'block';
        }

        previewButton.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            setStatus('', '');
            if (!fileInput.files.length) {
                setStatus('Selecione um arquivo XLSX antes do preview.', 'error');
                return;
            }

            const formData = new FormData();
            formData.append('file', fileInput.files[0]);

            previewButton.disabled = true;
            setStatus('Gerando preview...', '');
            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/fichas/import/preview', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    body: formData,
                    credentials: 'same-origin'
                });
                const data = await response.json();
                if (!data.success) {
                    setStatus(data.error || 'Falha ao gerar preview.', 'error');
                    resetPreview();
                } else {
                    currentToken = data.token;
                    currentColumns = data.columns || [];
                    previewTotal.textContent = data.counts ? data.counts.valid : 0;
                    previewInvalid.textContent = data.counts ? data.counts.invalid : 0;
                    const dupCount = data.counts ? (data.counts.duplicated_refs || 0) : 0;
                    document.getElementById('previewDup').textContent = dupCount;
                    document.getElementById('previewDupPill').style.display = dupCount > 0 ? '' : 'none';
                    renderMessages(data.messages || []);
                    renderColumnInfo(data.detected_columns, data.missing_columns, data.unmapped_columns);
                    renderInvalidDetails(data.invalid_rows);
                    renderPreview(currentColumns, data.preview_items || []);
                    // Disable confirm if there are errors (not just warnings)
                    const hasErrors = (data.messages || []).some(m => m.severity === 'error');
                    confirmButton.disabled = hasErrors;
                    if (hasErrors) {
                        setStatus('Preview gerado, mas há erros que impedem a importação.', 'error');
                    } else {
                        setStatus('Preview gerado com sucesso.', 'success');
                    }
                }
            } catch (err) {
                setStatus('Erro ao gerar preview.', 'error');
                resetPreview();
            } finally {
                previewButton.disabled = false;
            }
        });

        confirmButton.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            if (!currentToken) {
                setStatus('Gere o preview antes de confirmar.', 'error');
                return;
            }

            confirmButton.disabled = true;
            setStatus('Confirmando importacao...', '');
            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/fichas/import/confirm', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ token: currentToken }),
                    credentials: 'same-origin'
                });
                const data = await response.json();
                if (!data.success) {
                    setStatus(data.error || 'Falha ao confirmar importacao.', 'error');
                    confirmButton.disabled = false;
                    return;
                }
                setStatus('Importacao concluida. Redirecionando...', 'success');
                window.location.href = `/fichas/${data.ficha_id}/tabela`;
            } catch (err) {
                setStatus('Erro ao confirmar importacao.', 'error');
                confirmButton.disabled = false;
            }
        });

        clearButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
            fileInput.value = '';
            setStatus('', '');
            resetPreview();
        });
    </script>
</body>

</html>

        td {
            padding: 10px 12px;
            border-bottom: 1px solid #1f2937;
            color: #cbd5f5;
            text-align: left;
            white-space: nowrap;
        }

        th {
            font-weight: 600;
            color: #e2e8f0;
            cursor: pointer;
        }

        tr:hover td {
            background-color: #0f172a;
        }

        .pagination {
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            gap: 8px;
            margin-top: 16px;
        }

        .page-btn {
            padding: 8px 12px;
            background-color: #1e293b;
            color: #e5e7eb;
            border-radius: 6px;
            cursor: pointer;
            border: none;
        }

        .page-btn:disabled {
            opacity: 0.5;
            cursor: not-allowed;
        }

        .checkbox {
            width: 14px;
            height: 14px;
        }

        /* Flux button */
        .btn-flux {
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #7c3aed, #6d28d9);
            color: #fff;
        }

        .btn-flux:hover:not(:disabled) {
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6d28d9, #5b21b6);
        }

        .btn-flux:disabled {
            background: #1e293b;
            color: #475569;
            cursor: not-allowed;
        }

        .selection-counter {
            display: inline-flex;
            align-items: center;
            gap: 6px;
            font-size: 13px;
            color: #a78bfa;
            font-weight: 500;
            padding: 0 8px;
        }

        .selection-counter.hidden {
            display: none;
        }

        /* Modal overlay */
        .flux-modal-overlay {
            display: none;
            position: fixed;
            inset: 0;
            background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.7);
            backdrop-filter: blur(4px);
            z-index: 9999;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
        }

        .flux-modal-overlay.active {
            display: flex;
        }

        .flux-modal {
            background: #1e293b;
            border: 1px solid #334155;
            border-radius: 16px;
            padding: 32px;
            width: 480px;
            max-width: 90vw;
            max-height: 80vh;
            display: flex;
            flex-direction: column;
            box-shadow: 0 25px 50px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5);
        }

        .flux-modal-header {
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            gap: 12px;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
        }

        .flux-modal-header i {
            font-size: 24px;
            color: #a78bfa;
        }

        .flux-modal-header h2 {
            font-size: 20px;
            font-weight: 700;
            color: #fff;
            margin: 0;
        }

        .flux-modal-body {
            flex: 1;
            overflow-y: auto;
            margin-bottom: 24px;
        }

        .flux-modal-count {
            font-size: 15px;
            color: #cbd5e1;
            margin-bottom: 16px;
        }

        .flux-modal-count strong {
            color: #a78bfa;
        }

        .flux-item-list {
            list-style: none;
            padding: 0;
            margin: 0;
            max-height: 200px;
            overflow-y: auto;
            background: #0f172a;
            border-radius: 8px;
            border: 1px solid #1f2937;
        }

        .flux-item-list li {
            padding: 8px 12px;
            font-size: 12px;
            color: #94a3b8;
            border-bottom: 1px solid #1f2937;
            display: flex;
            gap: 8px;
        }

        .flux-item-list li:last-child {
            border-bottom: none;
        }

        .flux-item-list .item-ref {
            color: #e2e8f0;
            font-weight: 600;
            min-width: 100px;
        }

        .flux-modal-footer {
            display: flex;
            justify-content: flex-end;
            gap: 12px;
        }

        /* Result states */
        .flux-result-ok {
            color: #34d399;
        }

        .flux-result-fail {
            color: #f87171;
        }

        .flux-progress {
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            gap: 10px;
            padding: 12px;
            background: #0f172a;
            border-radius: 8px;
            color: #a78bfa;
            font-size: 14px;
        }

        .flux-spinner {
            width: 18px;
            height: 18px;
            border: 2px solid #334155;
            border-top-color: #a78bfa;
            border-radius: 50%;
            animation: fluxSpin 0.6s linear infinite;
        }

        @keyframes fluxSpin {
            to {
                transform: rotate(360deg);
            }
        }
    </style>
</head>

<body>
    <div class="app-container">
        <aside class="sidebar">
            <div class="logo">
                <img src="{{ url_for('static', filename='images/logo.png') }}" alt="Logo">
                <span>StyleFlow</span>
            </div>

            <nav class="nav-menu">
                <a href="{{ url_for('dashboard.index') }}" class="nav-item active">
                    <i class="fas fa-home"></i>
                    <span>Painel</span>
                </a>
                <a href="{{ url_for('collections.index') }}" class="nav-item">
                    <i class="fas fa-folder"></i>
                    <span>Minhas Colecoes</span>
                </a>
                <a href="{{ url_for('drawings.gallery') }}" class="nav-item">
                    <i class="fas fa-drafting-compass"></i>
                    <span>Desenhos Tecnicos</span>
                </a>
                <a href="{{ url_for('suppliers.index') }}" class="nav-item">
                    <i class="fas fa-truck"></i>
                    <span>Fornecedores</span>
                </a>
                <a href="{{ url_for('oaz_banco.import_view') }}" class="nav-item">
                    <i class="fas fa-database"></i>
                    <span>Banco OAZ</span>
                </a>
                <a href="#" class="nav-item">
                    <i class="fas fa-chart-line"></i>
                    <span>Relatorios</span>
                </a>
            </nav>

            <div style="margin-top: auto;">
                <a href="{{ url_for('settings.index') }}" class="nav-item">
                    <i class="fas fa-cog"></i>
                    <span>Configuracoes</span>
                </a>
                <a href="{{ url_for('auth.logout') }}" class="nav-item" style="color: #f87171;">
                    <i class="fas fa-sign-out-alt"></i>
                    <span>Sair</span>
                </a>

                <div class="user-profile">
                    <div class="user-avatar">
                        {{ current_user.username[0].upper() }}
                    </div>
                    <div class="user-info">
                        <div class="user-name">{{ current_user.username }}</div>
                        <div class="user-role">{% if current_user.is_admin %}Admin{% else %}Estilista{% endif %}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </aside>

        <main class="main-content">
            <header class="page-header">
                <div class="header-top">
                    <div>
                        <h1 class="page-title">Itens da Ficha Tecnica</h1>
                        <p class="page-subtitle">Gerencie os itens importados do Excel.</p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="action-group">
                        <button class="btn btn-danger" id="btnDeleteFicha" title="Excluir esta ficha inteira">
                            <i class="fas fa-trash-alt"></i>
                            Excluir Ficha
                        </button>
                        <a href="{{ url_for('dashboard.index') }}" class="btn btn-secondary">
                            <i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i>
                            Voltar
                        </a>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </header>

            <div class="controls">
                <div class="search-box">
                    <i class="fas fa-search"></i>
                    <input type="text" id="searchInput" placeholder="Buscar por referencia, descricao ou item">
                </div>
                <input class="select-input" type="text" id="filterGrupo" placeholder="Filtro grupo">
                <input class="select-input" type="text" id="filterLinha" placeholder="Filtro linha">
                <input class="select-input" type="text" id="filterCor" placeholder="Filtro cor">
                <select class="select-input" id="perPage">
                    <option value="25">25 por pagina</option>
                    <option value="50">50 por pagina</option>
                    <option value="100">100 por pagina</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <section class="table-card">
                <div class="table-actions">
                    <div class="action-group">
                        <label style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;">
                            <input type="checkbox" id="selectAll" class="checkbox">
                            Selecionar pagina
                        </label>
                        <button class="btn btn-danger" id="btnBulkDelete" disabled>
                            <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
                            Excluir selecionados
                        </button>
                        <button class="btn btn-ghost" id="btnClearAll">
                            <i class="fas fa-broom"></i>
                            Limpar tudo
                        </button>
                        <button class="btn btn-flux" id="btnSendFlux" disabled>
                            <i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i>
                            Enviar para o Flux
                        </button>
                        <span class="selection-counter hidden" id="selectionCounter">0 itens selecionados</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="action-group">
                        <button class="btn btn-primary" id="btnExport">
                            <i class="fas fa-file-export"></i>
                            Exportar CSV
                        </button>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="status-line" id="statusLine"></div>
                <div class="table-wrapper">
                    <table>
                        <thead>
                            <tr id="tableHeader"></tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody id="tableBody"></tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>
                <div class="pagination">
                    <button class="page-btn" id="prevPage">Anterior</button>
                    <button class="page-btn" id="nextPage">Proxima</button>
                </div>
            </section>
        </main>
    </div>

    <!-- Flux Confirmation Modal -->
    <div class="flux-modal-overlay" id="fluxModal">
        <div class="flux-modal">
            <div class="flux-modal-header">
                <i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i>
                <h2>Enviar para o Flux</h2>
            </div>
            <div class="flux-modal-body" id="fluxModalBody">
                <!-- Populated by JS -->
            </div>
            <div class="flux-modal-footer" id="fluxModalFooter">
                <button class="btn btn-secondary" id="btnFluxCancel">
                    <i class="fas fa-times"></i> Cancelar
                </button>
                <button class="btn btn-flux" id="btnFluxConfirm">
                    <i class="fas fa-check"></i> Confirmar envio
                </button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        const fichaId = {{ ficha.id }};
        const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
        const filterGrupo = document.getElementById('filterGrupo');
        const filterLinha = document.getElementById('filterLinha');
        const filterCor = document.getElementById('filterCor');
        const perPageSelect = document.getElementById('perPage');
        const selectAll = document.getElementById('selectAll');
        const btnBulkDelete = document.getElementById('btnBulkDelete');
        const btnClearAll = document.getElementById('btnClearAll');
        const btnExport = document.getElementById('btnExport');
        const btnSendFlux = document.getElementById('btnSendFlux');
        const selectionCounter = document.getElementById('selectionCounter');
        const fluxModal = document.getElementById('fluxModal');
        const fluxModalBody = document.getElementById('fluxModalBody');
        const btnFluxCancel = document.getElementById('btnFluxCancel');
        const btnFluxConfirm = document.getElementById('btnFluxConfirm');
        const statusLine = document.getElementById('statusLine');
        const tableHeader = document.getElementById('tableHeader');
        const tableBody = document.getElementById('tableBody');
        const prevPage = document.getElementById('prevPage');
        const nextPage = document.getElementById('nextPage');

        let columns = [];
        let currentPage = 1;
        let totalItems = 0;
        let selectedIds = new Set();
        let currentSort = 'item_no_ref_supplier';
        let currentOrder = 'asc';

        function setStatus(message, type) {
            statusLine.textContent = message || '';
            statusLine.className = 'status-line' + (type ? ' ' + type : '');
        }

        function buildHeader() {
            tableHeader.innerHTML = '';
            const selectTh = document.createElement('th');
            selectTh.textContent = '';
            tableHeader.appendChild(selectTh);

            columns.forEach(col => {
                const th = document.createElement('th');
                th.textContent = col.sourceColumnName || col.name;
                th.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    if (currentSort === col.name) {
                        currentOrder = currentOrder === 'asc' ? 'desc' : 'asc';
                    } else {
                        currentSort = col.name;
                        currentOrder = 'asc';
                    }
                    loadItems();
                });
                tableHeader.appendChild(th);
            });

            const actionTh = document.createElement('th');
            actionTh.textContent = 'Acoes';
            tableHeader.appendChild(actionTh);
        }

        function renderRows(items) {
            tableBody.innerHTML = '';
            items.forEach(item => {
                const tr = document.createElement('tr');
                const tdSelect = document.createElement('td');
                const checkbox = document.createElement('input');
                checkbox.type = 'checkbox';
                checkbox.className = 'checkbox';
                checkbox.dataset.id = item.id;
                checkbox.checked = selectedIds.has(item.id);
                checkbox.addEventListener('change', () => {
                    if (checkbox.checked) {
                        selectedIds.add(item.id);
                    } else {
                        selectedIds.delete(item.id);
                    }
                    updateBulkState();
                });
                tdSelect.appendChild(checkbox);
                tr.appendChild(tdSelect);

                columns.forEach(col => {
                    const td = document.createElement('td');
                    const value = item[col.name];
                    td.textContent = value === null || value === undefined ? '' : value;
                    tr.appendChild(td);
                });

                const tdAction = document.createElement('td');
                const editLink = document.createElement('a');
                editLink.href = `/fichas/${fichaId}/itens/${item.id}/editar`;
                editLink.className = 'btn btn-ghost';
                editLink.style.padding = '6px 10px';
                editLink.style.fontSize = '12px';
                editLink.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-edit"></i> Editar';
                tdAction.appendChild(editLink);
                tr.appendChild(tdAction);
                tableBody.appendChild(tr);
            });
            const checkboxes = tableBody.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
            const allChecked = checkboxes.length > 0 && Array.from(checkboxes).every(box => selectedIds.has(parseInt(box.dataset.id, 10)));
            selectAll.checked = allChecked;
        }

        function updateBulkState() {
            const hasSelection = selectedIds.size > 0;
            btnBulkDelete.disabled = !hasSelection;
            btnSendFlux.disabled = !hasSelection;
            if (hasSelection) {
                selectionCounter.classList.remove('hidden');
                selectionCounter.textContent = selectedIds.size === 1
                    ? '1 item selecionado'
                    : `${selectedIds.size} itens selecionados`;
            } else {
                selectionCounter.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        }

        async function loadColumns() {
            const response = await fetch(`/api/fichas/${fichaId}`, { credentials: 'same-origin' });
            const data = await response.json();
            if (!data.success) {
                setStatus(data.error || 'Falha ao carregar colunas.', 'error');
                return;
            }
            columns = data.columns || [];
            buildHeader();
            loadItems();
        }

        async function loadItems() {
            setStatus('Carregando itens...', '');
            const params = new URLSearchParams({
                page: currentPage,
                per_page: perPageSelect.value,
                q: searchInput.value.trim(),
                grupo: filterGrupo.value.trim(),
                linha: filterLinha.value.trim(),
                cor: filterCor.value.trim(),
                sort: currentSort,
                order: currentOrder
            });
            const response = await fetch(`/api/fichas/${fichaId}/itens?${params.toString()}`, { credentials: 'same-origin' });
            const data = await response.json();
            if (!data.success) {
                setStatus(data.error || 'Falha ao carregar itens.', 'error');
                return;
            }
            totalItems = data.total || 0;
            renderRows(data.items || []);
            updateBulkState();
            setStatus(`Total de itens: ${totalItems}`, 'success');
        }

        searchInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
            currentPage = 1;
            loadItems();
        });

        [filterGrupo, filterLinha, filterCor, perPageSelect].forEach(el => {
            el.addEventListener('change', () => {
                currentPage = 1;
                loadItems();
            });
        });

        selectAll.addEventListener('change', () => {
            const checkboxes = tableBody.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
            checkboxes.forEach(box => {
                const rowId = parseInt(box.dataset.id, 10);
                if (Number.isNaN(rowId)) {
                    return;
                }
                box.checked = selectAll.checked;
                if (selectAll.checked) {
                    selectedIds.add(rowId);
                } else {
                    selectedIds.delete(rowId);
                }
            });
            updateBulkState();
        });

        btnBulkDelete.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            if (!selectedIds.size) {
                return;
            }
            if (!confirm('Tem certeza que deseja excluir os itens selecionados?')) {
                return;
            }
            const response = await fetch(`/api/fichas/${fichaId}/itens/bulk-delete`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ ids: Array.from(selectedIds) }),
                credentials: 'same-origin'
            });
            const data = await response.json();
            if (!data.success) {
                setStatus(data.error || 'Falha ao excluir itens.', 'error');
                return;
            }
            selectedIds.clear();
            selectAll.checked = false;
            updateBulkState();
            setStatus('Itens excluidos.', 'success');
            loadItems();
        });

        btnClearAll.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            if (!confirm('Tem certeza que deseja limpar todos os itens da ficha?')) {
                return;
            }
            const response = await fetch(`/api/fichas/${fichaId}/itens/clear`, {
                method: 'POST',
                credentials: 'same-origin'
            });
            const data = await response.json();
            if (!data.success) {
                setStatus(data.error || 'Falha ao limpar itens.', 'error');
                return;
            }
            selectedIds.clear();
            selectAll.checked = false;
            updateBulkState();
            setStatus('Itens removidos.', 'success');
            loadItems();
        });

        btnExport.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const params = new URLSearchParams({
                export: 1,
                q: searchInput.value.trim(),
                grupo: filterGrupo.value.trim(),
                linha: filterLinha.value.trim(),
                cor: filterCor.value.trim(),
                sort: currentSort,
                order: currentOrder
            });
            window.location.href = `/api/fichas/${fichaId}/itens?${params.toString()}`;
        });

        // ─── Flux Send Flow ───

        // Cache item data for modal display
        let currentItemsCache = [];

        // Patch renderRows to also cache items for the modal
        const _origRenderRows = renderRows;
        renderRows = function (items) {
            currentItemsCache = items;
            _origRenderRows(items);
        };

        btnSendFlux.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (!selectedIds.size) return;
            showFluxConfirmation();
        });

        function showFluxConfirmation() {
            const count = selectedIds.size;
            const selectedItems = currentItemsCache.filter(it => selectedIds.has(it.id));

            let listHtml = '';
            if (selectedItems.length > 0) {
                const items = selectedItems.slice(0, 30);
                listHtml = '<ul class="flux-item-list">';
                items.forEach(it => {
                    const ref = it.oaz_reference || it.item_no_ref_supplier || `#${it.id}`;
                    const desc = it.nome_desc_produto || it.description_item || '';
                    listHtml += `<li><span class="item-ref">${ref}</span><span>${desc}</span></li>`;
                });
                if (selectedItems.length > 30) {
                    listHtml += `<li style="color:#64748b;">…e mais ${selectedItems.length - 30} itens</li>`;
                }
                listHtml += '</ul>';
            }

            fluxModalBody.innerHTML = `
                <p class="flux-modal-count">
                    Você está prestes a enviar <strong>${count}</strong>
                    ${count === 1 ? 'item' : 'itens'} desta ficha para o Fluxogama.
                </p>
                ${listHtml}
            `;

            btnFluxConfirm.disabled = false;
            btnFluxConfirm.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> Confirmar envio';
            btnFluxCancel.style.display = '';
            fluxModal.classList.add('active');
        }

        btnFluxCancel.addEventListener('click', () => {
            fluxModal.classList.remove('active');
        });

        // Close on overlay click
        fluxModal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target === fluxModal) fluxModal.classList.remove('active');
        });

        btnFluxConfirm.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            btnFluxConfirm.disabled = true;
            btnFluxConfirm.innerHTML = '<span class="flux-spinner"></span> Enviando…';
            btnFluxCancel.style.display = 'none';

            try {
                const resp = await fetch('/api/fluxogama/send-batch', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        ficha_id: fichaId,
                        item_ids: Array.from(selectedIds),
                    }),
                    credentials: 'same-origin',
                });

                const data = await resp.json();

                if (!resp.ok && !data.results) {
                    showFluxResult(null, data.error || 'Erro ao enviar.');
                    return;
                }

                showFluxResult(data, null);

                // Clear only IDs that succeeded; keep failures selected for retry
                if (data.results) {
                    data.results.forEach(r => {
                        if (r.ok) selectedIds.delete(r.item_id);
                    });
                    updateBulkState();
                    // Update checkbox visuals in the table
                    tableBody.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(box => {
                        const id = parseInt(box.dataset.id, 10);
                        box.checked = selectedIds.has(id);
                    });
                    selectAll.checked = false;
                }

                loadItems();
            } catch (err) {
                showFluxResult(null, `Erro de conexão: ${err.message}`);
            }
        });

        function showFluxResult(data, errorMsg) {
            let html = '';
            if (errorMsg) {
                html = `<p class="flux-result-fail"><i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i> ${errorMsg}</p>`;
            } else if (data) {
                const { success_count, error_count, results } = data;
                if (error_count === 0) {
                    html = `<p class="flux-result-ok"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> ${success_count} ${success_count === 1 ? 'item enviado' : 'itens enviados'} com sucesso!</p>`;
                } else {
                    html = `<p class="flux-result-ok" style="margin-bottom:8px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> ${success_count} enviado(s) com sucesso.</p>`;
                    html += `<p class="flux-result-fail" style="margin-bottom:12px;"><i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i> ${error_count} com erro.</p>`;
                }
                // Show per-item details
                if (results && results.length > 0) {
                    html += '<ul class="flux-item-list" style="margin-top:12px;">';
                    results.forEach(r => {
                        const icon = r.ok ? '<i class="fas fa-check" style="color:#34d399"></i>' : '<i class="fas fa-times" style="color:#f87171"></i>';
                        html += `<li>${icon} <span class="item-ref">Item #${r.item_id}</span><span>${r.message}</span></li>`;
                    });
                    html += '</ul>';
                }

                // Status line update
                if (error_count === 0) {
                    setStatus(`Envio concluído: ${success_count} itens enviados ao Flux.`, 'success');
                } else {
                    setStatus(`Envio parcial: ${success_count} OK, ${error_count} com erro.`, 'error');
                }
            }

            fluxModalBody.innerHTML = html;
            btnFluxConfirm.disabled = true;
            btnFluxConfirm.style.display = 'none';
            btnFluxCancel.style.display = '';
            btnFluxCancel.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-times"></i> Fechar';
        }

        prevPage.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (currentPage > 1) {
                currentPage -= 1;
                loadItems();
            }
        });

        nextPage.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const totalPages = Math.ceil(totalItems / parseInt(perPageSelect.value, 10));
            if (currentPage < totalPages) {
                currentPage += 1;
                loadItems();
            }
        });

        // ─── Delete entire ficha ───
        document.getElementById('btnDeleteFicha').addEventListener('click', async () => {
            if (!confirm('⚠️ Tem certeza que deseja EXCLUIR esta ficha inteira e todos os seus itens? Esta ação não pode ser desfeita.')) {
                return;
            }
            try {
                const resp = await fetch(`/api/fichas/${fichaId}`, {
                    method: 'DELETE',
                    credentials: 'same-origin',
                });
                const data = await resp.json();
                if (data.success) {
                    window.location.href = '{{ url_for("dashboard.index") }}';
                } else {
                    alert(data.error || 'Erro ao excluir ficha.');
                }
            } catch (err) {
                alert('Erro de conexão: ' + err.message);
            }
        });

        loadColumns();
    </script>
</body>

</html>


================================================================================
FILE: templates\login.html
================================================================================
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="pt-BR">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">

{% block content %}
<div class="row mt-4">
    <div class="col-12">
        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
            <h2><i class="fas fa-users me-2"></i>Gerenciar Usuários</h2>
            <a href="{{ url_for('admin.create_user') }}" class="btn btn-primary">
                <i class="fas fa-plus me-1"></i>Novo Usuário
            </a>
        </div>
        <hr>
    </div>
</div>

<div class="row">
    <div class="col-12">
        <div class="card">
            <div class="card-body">
                {% if users %}
                <div class="table-responsive">
                    <table class="table table-hover">
                        <thead>
                            <tr>
                                <th>ID</th>
                                <th>Nome de Usuário</th>
                                <th>E-mail</th>
                                <th>Tipo</th>
                                <th>Data Criação</th>
                                <th>Fichas</th>
                                <th>Ações</th>
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody>
                            {% for user in users %}
                            <tr>
                                <td>{{ user.id }}</td>
                                <td>
                                    <i class="fas fa-user me-1"></i>
                                    {{ user.username }}
                                </td>
                                <td>{{ user.email }}</td>
                                <td>
                                    {% if user.is_admin %}
                                        <span class="badge bg-danger">Admin</span>
                                    {% else %}
                                        <span class="badge bg-primary">Usuário</span>
                                    {% endif %}
                                </td>
                                <td>{{ user.created_at.strftime('%d/%m/%Y') }}</td>
                                <td>
                                    <span class="badge bg-info">{{ user.specifications|length }}</span>
                                </td>
                                <td>
                                    <div class="btn-group btn-group-sm">
                                        <a href="{{ url_for('admin.view_user', id=user.id) }}" class="btn btn-outline-primary" title="Ver detalhes">
                                            <i class="fas fa-eye"></i>
                                        </a>
                                        <a href="{{ url_for('admin.edit_user', id=user.id) }}" class="btn btn-outline-secondary" title="Editar">
                                            <i class="fas fa-edit"></i>
                                        </a>
                                        {% if not user.is_admin or user.id != session.user_id %}
                                        <button class="btn btn-outline-danger" title="Excluir usuário" 
                                                onclick="if(confirm('Tem certeza que deseja excluir o usuário {{ user.username }}? Todas as especificações deste usuário também serão excluídas.')) { 
                                                    document.getElementById('delete-user-form-{{ user.id }}').submit(); 
                                                }">
                                            <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
                                        </button>
                                        {% endif %}
                                    </div>
                                    {% if not user.is_admin or user.id != session.user_id %}
                                    <form id="delete-user-form-{{ user.id }}" method="POST" action="{{ url_for('admin.delete_user', id=user.id) }}" style="display: none;">
                                        <input type="hidden" name="csrf_token" value="{{ csrf_token() }}"/>
                                    </form>
                                    {% endif %}
                                </td>
                            </tr>
                            {% endfor %}
                        </tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>
                {% else %}
                <div class="text-center py-4">
                    <i class="fas fa-users fa-3x text-muted mb-3"></i>
                    <h5 class="text-muted">Nenhum usuário encontrado</h5>
                </div>
                {% endif %}
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>
{% endblock %}

<body>
    <div class="app-container">
        <!-- Sidebar -->
        <aside class="sidebar">

                        class="fas fa-sign-out-alt"></i><span>Sair</span></a>
                <div class="user-profile">
                    <div class="user-avatar">{{ session.get('username', 'A')[0].upper() if session.get('username') else
                        'A' }}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="user-name">{{ session.get('username', 'Admin') }}</div>
                        <div class="user-role">Administrador</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </aside>

        <!-- Main -->
        <main class="main-content">
            <header class="page-header">
                <div class="header-top">
                    <div>
                        <h1 class="page-title"><i class="fas fa-database" style="color: #3b82f6;"></i> Banco de Dados
                            OAZ</h1>
                        <p class="page-subtitle">Importe XLSX do Fluxogama para popular o De/Para de WSIDs.
                            <span class="admin-badge"><i class="fas fa-shield-alt"></i> Admin Only</span>

                    <a href="{{ url_for('dashboard.index') }}" class="btn btn-secondary"><i
                            class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i> Voltar</a>
                </div>
            </header>

            <!-- Current mapping stats -->
            <div class="stats-row">
                {% for key, label in field_options %}
                <div class="stat-box">
                    <div class="value">{{ mapping_counts.get(key, 0) }}</div>
                    <div class="label">{{ label }} ({{ key }})</div>
                </div>
                {% endfor %}
            </div>

            <!-- ═══ Step 1: Upload Card ═══ -->
            <div class="card" id="uploadCard">
                <div class="card-title"><i class="fas fa-upload"></i> Importar Banco de Dados</div>
                <p style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:13px;margin-bottom:16px">
                    <i class="fas fa-magic" style="color:#60a5fa"></i>
                    O tipo de banco (field_key) é detectado automaticamente pelo nome do arquivo.
                    Arraste vários arquivos de uma vez.
                </p>

                <div class="dropzone" id="dropzone">
                    <input type="file" id="fileInput" multiple accept=".xlsx">
                    <i class="fas fa-cloud-upload-alt"></i>
                    <h3>Arraste arquivos XLSX aqui</h3>
                    <p>ou clique para selecionar • Múltiplos arquivos aceitos • Máx. 50MB cada</p>
                </div>

                <div class="file-list" id="fileList"></div>

                <div class="btn-group">
                    <button class="btn btn-primary" id="btnPreview" disabled>
                        <i class="fas fa-search"></i> Preview
                    </button>
                    <button class="btn btn-secondary hidden" id="btnClear">
                        <i class="fas fa-times"></i> Limpar
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- ═══ Step 2: Preview Card ═══ -->
            <div class="card hidden" id="previewCard">
                <div class="card-title"><i class="fas fa-eye"></i> Preview da Importação</div>

                <!-- Preview stats -->
                <div class="preview-stats">
                    <div class="preview-stat total">
                        <div class="num" id="pvTotal">0</div>
                        <div class="lbl">Total de Linhas</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="preview-stat valid">
                        <div class="num" id="pvValid">0</div>
                        <div class="lbl">Válidas</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="preview-stat invalid">
                        <div class="num" id="pvInvalid">0</div>
                        <div class="lbl">Inválidas</div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <!-- Per-file results -->
                <div class="file-results" id="pvFiles"></div>

                <!-- Example rows: valid -->
                <div style="margin-top: 16px;">
                    <h4 style="color: #94a3b8; font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 8px; text-transform: uppercase;">
                        <i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color:#34d399"></i> Exemplos válidos (até 10)
                    </h4>
                    <table class="preview-table">
                        <thead>
                            <tr>
                                <th>#</th>
                                <th>Descrição</th>
                                <th>text_norm</th>
                                <th>WSID</th>
                                <th>Arquivo</th>
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody id="pvExamples"></tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>

                <!-- Example rows: invalid -->
                <div style="margin-top: 16px;" id="pvInvalidSection" class="hidden">
                    <h4 style="color: #94a3b8; font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 8px; text-transform: uppercase;">
                        <i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle" style="color:#f87171"></i> Exemplos inválidos (até 10)
                    </h4>
                    <table class="preview-table">
                        <thead>
                            <tr>
                                <th>#</th>
                                <th>Descrição</th>
                                <th>WSID</th>
                                <th>Motivo</th>
                                <th>Arquivo</th>
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody id="pvInvalidExamples"></tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>

                <div class="btn-group">
                    <button class="btn btn-success" id="btnConfirm">
                        <i class="fas fa-check"></i> Confirmar Importação
                    </button>
                    <button class="btn btn-secondary" id="btnBackToUpload">
                        <i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i> Voltar
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- ═══ Step 3: Progress Card ═══ -->
            <div class="card hidden" id="progressCard">
                <div class="card-title"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> <span
                        id="progressTitle">Importando...</span></div>

                <table class="progress-table">
                    <thead>
                        <tr>
                            <th>#</th>
                            <th>Arquivo</th>
                            <th>Tipo</th>
                            <th>Linhas</th>
                            <th>Válidos</th>

                    </thead>
                    <tbody id="progressBody"></tbody>

                <div class="summary-bar hidden" id="summaryBar">
                    <div class="item">
                        <div class="num" id="sumCreated">0</div>
                        <div class="lbl">Criados</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="item">
                        <div class="num" id="sumUpdated">0</div>
                        <div class="lbl">Atualizados</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="item">
                        <div class="num" id="sumTotal">0</div>
                        <div class="lbl">Total</div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="btn-group hidden" id="doneActions">

    <script src="{{ url_for('static', filename='js/toast.js') }}"></script>
    <script>
        // ── DOM refs ────────────────────────────────────────────────
        const dropzone = document.getElementById('dropzone');
        const fileInput = document.getElementById('fileInput');
        const fileList = document.getElementById('fileList');
        const btnPreview = document.getElementById('btnPreview');
        const btnClear = document.getElementById('btnClear');
        const btnConfirm = document.getElementById('btnConfirm');
        const btnBackToUpload = document.getElementById('btnBackToUpload');

        // Field key options for manual override dropdowns
        const FIELD_OPTIONS = [
            {% for key, label in field_options %}
        { key: '{{ key }}', label: '{{ label }}' },
        {% endfor %}
        ];

        let selectedFiles = [];
        let previewToken = null;
        let previewData = null;  // store for overrides

        // ── Step 1: File Upload ─────────────────────────────────────
        dropzone.addEventListener('dragover', e => { e.preventDefault(); dropzone.classList.add('drag-over'); });
        dropzone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => dropzone.classList.remove('drag-over'));
        dropzone.addEventListener('drop', e => {
            e.preventDefault();
            dropzone.classList.remove('drag-over');
            addFiles(e.dataTransfer.files);
        });
        fileInput.addEventListener('change', () => addFiles(fileInput.files));

        function addFiles(files) {
            for (const f of files) {
                if (!f.name.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xlsx')) continue;
                if (selectedFiles.some(sf => sf.name === f.name)) continue;
                selectedFiles.push(f);
            }
            renderFileList();
        }

        function renderFileList() {
            fileList.innerHTML = '';
            selectedFiles.forEach((f, idx) => {
                const size = (f.size / 1024).toFixed(1);
                fileList.innerHTML += `
                    <div class="file-item">
                        <i class="fas fa-file-excel file-icon"></i>
                        <span class="file-name">${f.name}</span>
                        <span class="file-size">${size} KB</span>
                        <button class="remove-btn" onclick="removeFile(${idx})"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>
                    </div>`;
            });
            btnClear.classList.toggle('hidden', selectedFiles.length === 0);
            btnPreview.disabled = selectedFiles.length === 0;
        }

        function removeFile(idx) {
            selectedFiles.splice(idx, 1);
            renderFileList();
        }

        btnClear.addEventListener('click', () => { selectedFiles = []; renderFileList(); });

        // ── Step 2: Preview ─────────────────────────────────────────
        btnPreview.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            if (selectedFiles.length === 0) return;
            btnPreview.disabled = true;
            btnPreview.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Analisando...';

            const formData = new FormData();
            selectedFiles.forEach(f => formData.append('files[]', f));

            try {
                const resp = await fetch('/api/admin/bancos/preview', { method: 'POST', body: formData });
                const data = await resp.json();

                if (!data.success) {
                    toast(data.error, 'error');
                    btnPreview.disabled = false;
                    btnPreview.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-search"></i> Preview';
                    return;
                }

                previewToken = data.token;
                previewData = data;
                showPreview(data);
            } catch (err) {
                toast('Erro de rede: ' + err.message, 'error');
                btnPreview.disabled = false;
                btnPreview.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-search"></i> Preview';
            }
        });

        function buildOverrideSelect(filename) {
            let opts = '<option value="">-- Selecione --</option>';
            FIELD_OPTIONS.forEach(o => {
                opts += `<option value="${o.key}">${o.label} (${o.key})</option>`;
            });
            return `<select class="form-select" style="font-size:12px;padding:4px 8px;background:#0f1420;color:#e2e8f0;border:1px solid #f87171;border-radius:6px;max-width:220px" data-override-for="${esc(filename)}">${opts}</select>`;
        }

        function showPreview(data) {
            document.getElementById('uploadCard').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('previewCard').classList.remove('hidden');

            // Stats
            document.getElementById('pvTotal').textContent = data.total_rows;
            document.getElementById('pvValid').textContent = data.total_valid;
            document.getElementById('pvInvalid').textContent = data.total_invalid;

            // Per-file results with auto-detect info
            const pvFiles = document.getElementById('pvFiles');
            pvFiles.innerHTML = '';
            let hasUndetected = false;
            (data.files || []).forEach(f => {
                // Build detected columns string
                const dc = f.detected_columns || {};
                const cols = [];
                if (dc.wsid) cols.push(`WSID → "${dc.wsid}"`);
                if (dc.codigo) cols.push(`Código → "${dc.codigo}"`);
                if (dc.descricao) cols.push(`Descrição → "${dc.descricao}"`);
                if (dc.status) cols.push(`Status → "${dc.status}"`);
                const colsStr = cols.length ? cols.join(' · ') : '';

                // Field key detection badge
                let fkBadge;
                if (f.field_key) {
                    const src = f.detect_source === 'filename' ? 'nome do arquivo' : (f.detect_source === 'sheet_name' ? 'aba da planilha' : 'override');
                    fkBadge = `<span class="badge badge-done" style="font-size:11px">${f.field_key} — ${f.field_key_label}</span>
                               <span style="font-size:10px;color:#94a3b8;margin-left:4px">(via ${src})</span>`;
                } else {
                    hasUndetected = true;
                    fkBadge = `<span class="badge badge-error" style="font-size:11px">Não detectado</span>
                               <span style="margin-left:8px">${buildOverrideSelect(f.filename)}</span>`;
                }

                pvFiles.innerHTML += `
                    <div class="file-result-item" style="flex-wrap:wrap;gap:8px">
                        <div style="flex:1;min-width:200px">
                            <div class="fname"><i class="fas fa-file-excel" style="color:#22c55e;margin-right:8px"></i>${f.filename}</div>
                            <div class="fmeta">Planilha: ${f.sheet_name || '-'} · ${f.total_rows} linhas · ${f.valid_items} válidas · ${f.skipped_invalid || 0} inválidas</div>
                            ${colsStr ? `<div class="fmeta" style="margin-top:4px;color:#60a5fa"><i class="fas fa-columns" style="margin-right:4px"></i>${colsStr}</div>` : ''}
                        </div>
                        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">
                            ${fkBadge}
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
            });

            // Valid example rows
            const tbody = document.getElementById('pvExamples');
            tbody.innerHTML = '';
            (data.examples_valid || []).forEach((ex, i) => {
                tbody.innerHTML += `<tr>
                    <td>${i + 1}</td>
                    <td>${esc(ex.descricao)}</td>
                    <td class="text-muted">${esc(ex.text_norm)}</td>
                    <td class="wsid-col">${esc(ex.wsid)}</td>
                    <td class="text-muted">${esc(ex.source)}</td>
                </tr>`;
            });

            if (!data.examples_valid || data.examples_valid.length === 0) {
                tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" style="text-align:center;color:#64748b">Nenhum item válido encontrado</td></tr>';
            }

            // Enable confirm only if there are importable files
            btnConfirm.disabled = !(data.total_importable > 0);

            // Invalid example rows
            const invSection = document.getElementById('pvInvalidSection');
            const invBody = document.getElementById('pvInvalidExamples');
            invBody.innerHTML = '';
            if (data.examples_invalid && data.examples_invalid.length > 0) {
                invSection.classList.remove('hidden');
                data.examples_invalid.forEach((ex, i) => {
                    invBody.innerHTML += `<tr>
                        <td>${i + 1}</td>
                        <td>${esc(ex.descricao) || '<em style="color:#64748b">vazio</em>'}</td>
                        <td class="wsid-col">${esc(ex.wsid) || '<em style="color:#64748b">vazio</em>'}</td>
                        <td style="color:#f87171">${esc(ex.reason)}</td>
                        <td class="text-muted">${esc(ex.source)}</td>
                    </tr>`;
                });
            } else {
                invSection.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        }

        btnBackToUpload.addEventListener('click', () => {
            document.getElementById('previewCard').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('uploadCard').classList.remove('hidden');
            btnPreview.disabled = false;
            btnPreview.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-search"></i> Preview';
            previewToken = null;
            previewData = null;
        });

        // ── Step 3: Confirm ─────────────────────────────────────────
        btnConfirm.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            if (!previewToken) return;
            btnConfirm.disabled = true;
            btnConfirm.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Gravando...';

            // Collect overrides from manual selectors
            const overrides = {};
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-override-for]').forEach(sel => {
                if (sel.value) overrides[sel.dataset.overrideFor] = sel.value;
            });

            try {
                const resp = await fetch('/api/admin/bancos/confirm', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ token: previewToken, overrides }),
                });
                const data = await resp.json();

                if (!data.success) {
                    toast(data.error, 'error');
                    btnConfirm.disabled = false;
                    btnConfirm.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> Confirmar Importação';
                    return;
                }

                document.getElementById('previewCard').classList.add('hidden');
                startPolling(data.job_id);
            } catch (err) {
                toast('Erro: ' + err.message, 'error');
                btnConfirm.disabled = false;
                btnConfirm.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> Confirmar Importação';
            }
        });

        // ── Polling ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
        function startPolling(jobId) {
            const card = document.getElementById('progressCard');
            card.classList.remove('hidden');

            const poll = async () => {
                try {
                    const resp = await fetch(`/api/admin/bancos/status/${jobId}`);
                    const data = await resp.json();
                    if (!data.success) return;

                    updateProgress(data);

                    if (data.status === 'done') {
                        document.getElementById('progressTitle').innerHTML =
                            '<i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color:#34d399"></i> Importação concluída!';
                        const spinner = document.querySelector('#progressCard .card-title .fa-spinner');
                        if (spinner) spinner.remove();
                        document.getElementById('summaryBar').classList.remove('hidden');
                        document.getElementById('sumCreated').textContent = data.total_created;
                        document.getElementById('sumUpdated').textContent = data.total_updated;
                        document.getElementById('sumTotal').textContent = data.total_created + data.total_updated;
                        document.getElementById('doneActions').classList.remove('hidden');
                        return;
                    }
                    setTimeout(poll, 1000);
                } catch { setTimeout(poll, 2000); }
            };
            poll();
        }

        function updateProgress(data) {
            const tbody = document.getElementById('progressBody');
            let html = '';
            (data.files || []).forEach((f, i) => {
                const statusBadge = {
                    queued: '<span class="badge badge-queued">Aguardando</span>',
                    processing: '<span class="badge badge-processing">Processando</span>',
                    done: '<span class="badge badge-done">Concluído</span>',
                    error: '<span class="badge badge-error">Erro</span>',
                    empty: '<span class="badge badge-empty">Vazio</span>',
                    partial: '<span class="badge badge-partial">Parcial</span>',
                }[f.status] || `<span class="badge badge-queued">${f.status}</span>`;

                const isActive = data.status === 'processing' && i === data.current_file_index;
                const rowStyle = isActive ? 'background: rgba(59,130,246,0.08);' : '';

                html += `<tr style="${rowStyle}">
                    <td>${i + 1}</td>
                    <td>${f.filename || ''}</td>
                    <td><span style="color:#60a5fa;font-size:12px">${f.field_key || '?'}</span> <span style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px">${f.field_key_label || ''}</span></td>
                    <td>${f.total_rows ?? '-'}</td>
                    <td>${f.valid_items ?? '-'}</td>
                    <td>${f.created ?? '-'}</td>
                    <td>${f.updated ?? '-'}</td>
                    <td>${statusBadge}${f.error ? `<br><small style="color:#f87171">${f.error}</small>` : ''}</td>
                </tr>`;
            });
            tbody.innerHTML = html;
        }

        // ── Utils ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
        function esc(s) {
            if (!s) return '';
            const d = document.createElement('div');
            d.textContent = s;
            return d.innerHTML;
        }

        function toast(msg, type) {
            if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast(msg, type);
            else alert(msg);
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>

FILE: templates\settings.html
================================================================================

            transition: all 0.2s;
            cursor: pointer;
        }

        .nav-item:hover {
            background-color: #1e293b;
            color: #e5e7eb;
        }

        .nav-item.active {
            background-color: #2563eb;
            color: #ffffff;
        }

        .nav-item i {
            width: 20px;
            text-align: center;
        }

        /* Settings Menu in Sidebar */
        .settings-menu {
            border-top: 1px solid #1e293b;
            padding-top: 16px;
            margin-top: 16px;
        }

        .settings-menu-item {
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            gap: 12px;
            padding: 10px 16px;
            margin-bottom: 4px;
            border-radius: 8px;
            color: #94a3b8;
            text-decoration: none;
            transition: all 0.2s;

        }

        }

        /* User Profile */
        .user-profile {
            display: flex;

            gap: 12px;

        }

        .user-avatar {
            width: 40px;

            border-radius: 50%;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%);
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            justify-content: center;
            color: white;
            font-weight: 600;
        }

        .user-info {
            flex: 1;
        }

        .user-name {

                    </div>

            </div>
        </aside>

        <main class="main-content">
            <header class="page-header">
                <div class="header-top">

                        <p class="page-subtitle">Gerencie seus contatos e parcerias de forma eficiente</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </header>

            {% with messages = get_flashed_messages() %}
            {% if messages %}
            {% for message in messages %}
            <div class="flash-message success">
                <i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i>
                <span>{{ message }}</span>
            </div>
            {% endfor %}
            {% endif %}
            {% endwith %}

            <div class="search-bar">
                <div class="search-input-group">
                    <i class="fas fa-search"></i>
                    <input type="text" id="searchInput" placeholder="Buscar fornecedor..." value="{{ search_query }}">
                </div>
                <div class="material-filter-group">
                    <select id="materialFilter">
                        <option value="">Todos os materiais</option>
                        {% for material in materials_options %}
                        <option value="{{ material }}" {{ 'selected' if material==material_filter else '' }}>
                            {{ material }}
                        </option>
                        {% endfor %}
                    </select>
                </div>
                <button class="btn-primary" onclick="openModal()">
                    <i class="fas fa-plus"></i>
                    Novo Fornecedor
                </button>

            <div class="suppliers-table">
                <div class="table-header">
                    <div>FORNECEDOR</div>

                    <div>PEÇAS ASSOCIADAS</div>
                    <div>AÇÕES</div>
                </div>

                {% for item in suppliers %}
                <div class="table-row">
                    <div class="supplier-info">
                        <div class="supplier-avatar" style="background-color: {{ item.supplier.avatar_color }};">
                            {{ item.supplier.name[0].upper() }}
                        </div>
                        <div class="supplier-details">
                            <h4>{{ item.supplier.name }}</h4>
                            <p>{{ item.supplier.location or 'Localização não informada' }}</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <div class="contact-info">
                        <p>{{ item.supplier.contact_name or 'Sem contato' }}</p>
                        <span>{{ item.supplier.contact_email or '' }}</span>
                    </div>

                    <div class="materials-tags">
                        {% if item.supplier.materials_json %}
                        {% set materials_list = item.supplier.materials_json | from_json %}
                        {% for material in materials_list[:3] %}
                        <span class="material-tag" style="background-color: {{ material.color }}; color: white;">
                            {{ material.name }}
                        </span>
                        {% endfor %}
                        {% if materials_list | length > 3 %}
                        <span class="material-tag" style="background-color: #64748b; color: white;">
                            +{{ materials_list | length - 3 }}

                            <i class="fas fa-ellipsis-h"></i>

                            <i class="fas fa-edit"></i>

                            onclick="deleteSupplier({{ item.supplier.id }}, '{{ item.supplier.name }}')">

            {% if pagination.pages > 1 %}

                    class="page-btn {{ 'active' if page_num == pagination.page else '' }}">

    <div id="supplierModal" class="modal">
        <div class="modal-content">
            <div class="modal-header">
                <h2 id="modalTitle">Novo Fornecedor</h2>
                <button class="close-btn" onclick="closeModal()">&times;</button>
            </div>

            <form id="supplierForm" onsubmit="saveSupplier(event)">
                <input type="hidden" id="supplierId">

                <div class="form-group">
                    <label>Nome do Fornecedor *</label>
                    <input type="text" id="supplierName" required>
                </div>

                <div class="form-group">
                    <label>Localização</label>
                    <input type="text" id="supplierLocation" placeholder="Ex: São Paulo, SP">
                </div>

                <div class="form-group">
                    <label>Nome do Contato</label>
                    <input type="text" id="contactName">
                </div>

                <div class="form-group">
                    <label>E-mail do Contato</label>
                    <input type="email" id="contactEmail">
                </div>

                <div class="form-group">
                    <label>Telefone do Contato</label>
                    <input type="tel" id="contactPhone">
                </div>

                <div class="form-group">
                    <label>Materiais Fornecidos</label>
                    <div class="materials-input" id="materialsContainer"></div>
                    <div class="add-material-form">
                        <input type="text" id="newMaterialName" placeholder="Nome do material">
                        <select id="newMaterialColor">
                            <option value="#6366f1">Roxo</option>
                            <option value="#10b981">Verde</option>
                            <option value="#3b82f6">Azul</option>
                            <option value="#f59e0b">Laranja</option>
                            <option value="#ef4444">Vermelho</option>
                            <option value="#8b5cf6">Violeta</option>
                            <option value="#ec4899">Rosa</option>
                            <option value="#14b8a6">Teal</option>
                        </select>
                        <button type="button" onclick="addMaterial()">Adicionar</button>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="form-group">
                    <label>Cor do Avatar</label>
                    <div class="avatar-colors">
                        <div class="avatar-color-option selected" style="background-color: #667eea;"
                            data-color="#667eea"></div>
                        <div class="avatar-color-option" style="background-color: #f093fb;" data-color="#f093fb"></div>
                        <div class="avatar-color-option" style="background-color: #4facfe;" data-color="#4facfe"></div>
                        <div class="avatar-color-option" style="background-color: #43e97b;" data-color="#43e97b"></div>
                        <div class="avatar-color-option" style="background-color: #fa709a;" data-color="#fa709a"></div>
                        <div class="avatar-color-option" style="background-color: #ff9a56;" data-color="#ff9a56"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <button type="submit" class="btn-save">Salvar Fornecedor</button>
            </form>
