    <div id="productsModal" class="modal">
        <div class="modal-content">
            <div class="modal-header">
                <h2 id="productsModalTitle">Produtos do Fornecedor</h2>
                <button class="close-btn" onclick="closeProductsModal()">&times;</button>
            </div>
            <div id="productsModalBody">
                <p>Carregando...</p>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let materials = [];
        let selectedColor = '#667eea';
        let currentSupplierId = null;

        // Search functionality
        document.getElementById('searchInput').addEventListener('keyup', function (e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                const searchValue = this.value;
                const materialValue = document.getElementById('materialFilter').value;
                window.location.href = `?search=${encodeURIComponent(searchValue)}&material=${encodeURIComponent(materialValue)}`;
            }
        });

        document.getElementById('materialFilter').addEventListener('change', function () {
            const searchValue = document.getElementById('searchInput').value;
            const materialValue = this.value;
            window.location.href = `?search=${encodeURIComponent(searchValue)}&material=${encodeURIComponent(materialValue)}`;
        });

        // Avatar color selection
        document.querySelectorAll('.avatar-color-option').forEach(option => {
            option.addEventListener('click', function () {
                document.querySelectorAll('.avatar-color-option').forEach(opt => opt.classList.remove('selected'));
                this.classList.add('selected');
                selectedColor = this.dataset.color;
            });
        });

        function openModal() {
            document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = 'Novo Fornecedor';
            document.getElementById('supplierForm').reset();
            document.getElementById('supplierId').value = '';
            materials = [];
            renderMaterials();
            currentSupplierId = null;
            document.getElementById('supplierModal').classList.add('show');
        }

        function closeModal() {
            document.getElementById('supplierModal').classList.remove('show');
        }

        function addMaterial() {
            const name = document.getElementById('newMaterialName').value.trim();
            const color = document.getElementById('newMaterialColor').value;

            if (name) {
                materials.push({ name, color });
                document.getElementById('newMaterialName').value = '';
                renderMaterials();
            }
        }

        function removeMaterial(index) {
            materials.splice(index, 1);
            renderMaterials();
        }

        function renderMaterials() {
            const container = document.getElementById('materialsContainer');
            container.innerHTML = materials.map((material, index) => `
                <div class="material-chip" style="background-color: ${material.color}">
                    ${material.name}
                    <button type="button" onclick="removeMaterial(${index})">×</button>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        }

        async function saveSupplier(e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            const data = {
                name: document.getElementById('supplierName').value,
                location: document.getElementById('supplierLocation').value,
                contact_name: document.getElementById('contactName').value,
                contact_email: document.getElementById('contactEmail').value,
                contact_phone: document.getElementById('contactPhone').value,
                materials: materials,
                avatar_color: selectedColor
            };

            try {
                const url = currentSupplierId
                    ? `/suppliers/${currentSupplierId}/update`
                    : '/suppliers/create';

                const response = await fetch(url, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                        'X-CSRFToken': '{{ csrf_token() }}'
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify(data)
                });

                const result = await response.json();

                if (result.success) {
                    window.location.reload();
                } else {
                    alert('Erro: ' + result.message);
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error:', error);
                alert('Erro ao salvar fornecedor');
            }
        }

        async function editSupplier(id) {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/suppliers/${id}`);
                const supplier = await response.json();

                document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = 'Editar Fornecedor';
                document.getElementById('supplierId').value = supplier.id;
                document.getElementById('supplierName').value = supplier.name;
                document.getElementById('supplierLocation').value = supplier.location || '';
                document.getElementById('contactName').value = supplier.contact_name || '';
                document.getElementById('contactEmail').value = supplier.contact_email || '';
                document.getElementById('contactPhone').value = supplier.contact_phone || '';

                materials = supplier.materials || [];
                renderMaterials();

                selectedColor = supplier.avatar_color;
                document.querySelectorAll('.avatar-color-option').forEach(opt => {
                    opt.classList.toggle('selected', opt.dataset.color === selectedColor);
                });

                currentSupplierId = id;
                document.getElementById('supplierModal').classList.add('show');
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error:', error);
                alert('Erro ao carregar fornecedor');
            }
        }

        function closeProductsModal() {
            document.getElementById('productsModal').classList.remove('show');
        }

        function formatProductStatus(status) {
            const normalized = (status || '').toLowerCase();
            if (normalized === 'completed') {
                return 'Concluido';
            }
            if (normalized === 'in_development') {
                return 'Em desenvolvimento';
            }
            if (normalized === 'approved') {
                return 'Aprovado';
            }
            return 'Rascunho';
        }

        async function viewSupplierProducts(id) {
            const modal = document.getElementById('productsModal');
            const body = document.getElementById('productsModalBody');
            const title = document.getElementById('productsModalTitle');

            modal.classList.add('show');
            body.innerHTML = '<p>Carregando...</p>';
            title.textContent = 'Produtos do fornecedor';

            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/suppliers/${id}/products`);
                const data = await response.json();

                if (!data.success) {
                    body.innerHTML = '<p>Erro ao carregar produtos.</p>';
                    return;
                }

                title.textContent = `Produtos de ${data.supplier_name || 'Fornecedor'}`;

                if (!data.products || data.products.length === 0) {
                    body.innerHTML = '<p>Nenhum produto associado.</p>';
                    return;
                }

                const itemsHtml = data.products.map(product => {
                    const thumbHtml = product.thumbnail
                        ? `<img src="${product.thumbnail}" alt="">`
                        : '<i class="fas fa-file"></i>';
                    const refLabel = product.ref ? `Ref: ${product.ref}` : 'Ref: -';
                    const statusLabel = formatProductStatus(product.status);
                    const nameLabel = product.name || 'Produto';
                    return `
                        <div class="product-item">
                            <div class="product-thumb">${thumbHtml}</div>
                            <div class="product-meta">
                                <h4>${nameLabel}</h4>
                                <span>${refLabel}</span>
                                <span>Status: ${statusLabel}</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    `;
                }).join('');

                body.innerHTML = `<div class="products-list">${itemsHtml}</div>`;
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error:', error);
                body.innerHTML = '<p>Erro ao carregar produtos.</p>';
            }
        }

        async function deleteSupplier(id, name) {
            if (confirm(`Tem certeza que deseja excluir o fornecedor "${name}"?\n\nEsta ação não pode ser desfeita.`)) {
                try {
                    const response = await fetch(`/suppliers/${id}/delete`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: {
                            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                            'X-CSRFToken': '{{ csrf_token() }}'
                        }
                    });

                    const result = await response.json();

                    if (result.success) {
                        window.location.reload();
                    } else {
                        alert('Erro: ' + result.message);
                    }
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('Error:', error);
                    alert('Erro ao excluir fornecedor');
                }
            }
        }

        function viewSupplier(id) {
            editSupplier(id);
        }

        window.onclick = function (event) {
            const modal = document.getElementById('supplierModal');
            const productsModal = document.getElementById('productsModal');
            if (event.target == modal) {
                closeModal();
            }
            if (event.target == productsModal) {
                closeProductsModal();
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>

    <script>
        function openDrawingModal(imageUrl, title, specId) {
            const modal = document.getElementById('drawingModal');
            const modalImage = document.getElementById('modalImage');
            const modalTitle = document.getElementById('modalTitle');
            const modalDetailsBtn = document.getElementById('modalDetailsBtn');

            modalImage.src = imageUrl;
            modalTitle.textContent = title;
            modalDetailsBtn.href = `/specification/${specId}`;

            modal.classList.add('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'; // Prevent background scrolling
        }

        function closeDrawingModal() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('drawingModal');
            modal.classList.remove('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'auto'; // Restore scrolling
        }

        // Close modal with ESC key
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {
            if (event.key === 'Escape') {
                closeDrawingModal();
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>

<div class="container-fluid py-4">

                <div class="card-body">
                    <form id="batchUploadForm">

                                <i class="fas fa-cloud-upload-alt fa-3x text-muted mb-3"></i>
                                <p class="mb-2">Arraste arquivos aqui ou clique para selecionar</p>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const dropZone = document.getElementById('dropZone');
    const fileInput = document.getElementById('fileInput');
    const fileList = document.getElementById('fileList');
    const fileListItems = document.getElementById('fileListItems');
    const fileCount = document.getElementById('fileCount');
    const uploadBtn = document.getElementById('uploadBtn');
    const clearBtn = document.getElementById('clearBtn');
    const form = document.getElementById('batchUploadForm');
    const progressSection = document.getElementById('progressSection');
    
    let selectedFiles = [];
    let currentBatchId = null;
    let statusInterval = null;
    
    dropZone.addEventListener('click', () => fileInput.click());
    
    dropZone.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        dropZone.classList.add('border-primary');
    });
    
    dropZone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
        dropZone.classList.remove('border-primary');
    });
    
    dropZone.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        dropZone.classList.remove('border-primary');
        handleFiles(e.dataTransfer.files);
    });
    
    fileInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
        handleFiles(e.target.files);
    });
    
    function handleFiles(files) {
        for (let file of files) {
            const ext = file.name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            if (['pdf', 'jpg', 'jpeg', 'png'].includes(ext)) {
                if (!selectedFiles.find(f => f.name === file.name && f.size === file.size)) {
                    selectedFiles.push(file);
                }
            }
        }
        updateFileList();
    }
    
    function updateFileList() {
        if (selectedFiles.length > 0) {
            fileList.style.display = 'block';
            clearBtn.style.display = 'inline-block';
            uploadBtn.disabled = false;
            fileCount.textContent = selectedFiles.length;
            
            fileListItems.innerHTML = selectedFiles.map((file, index) => `
                <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center py-2 px-3 border-bottom border-secondary">
                    <div>
                        <i class="fas fa-file-${file.name.endsWith('.pdf') ? 'pdf text-danger' : 'image text-info'} me-2"></i>
                        <span>${file.name}</span>
                        <small class="text-muted ms-2">(${(file.size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2)} MB)</small>
                    </div>
                    <button type="button" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger" onclick="removeFile(${index})">
                        <i class="fas fa-times"></i>
                    </button>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        } else {
            fileList.style.display = 'none';
            clearBtn.style.display = 'none';
            uploadBtn.disabled = true;
        }
    }
    
    window.removeFile = function(index) {
        selectedFiles.splice(index, 1);
        updateFileList();
    };
    
    clearBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        selectedFiles = [];
        fileInput.value = '';
        updateFileList();
    });
    
    form.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        
        if (selectedFiles.length === 0) return;
        
        uploadBtn.disabled = true;
        uploadBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin me-2"></i>Enviando...';
        
        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('csrf_token', document.querySelector('[name="csrf_token"]').value);
        formData.append('collection_id', document.querySelector('[name="collection_id"]').value);
        formData.append('supplier_id', document.querySelector('[name="supplier_id"]').value);
        formData.append('stylist', document.querySelector('[name="stylist"]').value);
        formData.append('price_range', document.querySelector('[name="price_range"]').value);
        
        for (let file of selectedFiles) {
            formData.append('files', file);
        }
        
        try {
            const response = await fetch('{{ url_for("specifications.upload_batch_files") }}', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            });
            
            const data = await response.json();
            
            if (data.success) {
                currentBatchId = data.batch_id;
                progressSection.style.display = 'block';
                uploadBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check me-2"></i>Enviado!';
                
                startStatusPolling();
            } else {
                alert('Erro: ' + (data.error || 'Falha no upload'));
                uploadBtn.disabled = false;
                uploadBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-upload me-2"></i>Iniciar Upload';
            }
        } catch (error) {
            alert('Erro de conexao: ' + error.message);
            uploadBtn.disabled = false;
            uploadBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-upload me-2"></i>Iniciar Upload';
        }
    });
    
    function startStatusPolling() {
        updateStatus();
        statusInterval = setInterval(updateStatus, 2000);
    }
    
    async function updateStatus() {
        if (!currentBatchId) return;
        
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`/batch_status/${currentBatchId}`);
            const data = await response.json();
            
            if (data.success) {
                document.getElementById('progressBar').style.width = data.progress_percent + '%';
                document.getElementById('progressBar').textContent = data.progress_percent + '%';
                
                document.getElementById('badgePending').textContent = data.pending + ' Aguardando';
                document.getElementById('badgeProcessing').textContent = data.processing + ' Processando';
                document.getElementById('badgeCompleted').textContent = data.completed + ' Concluido';
                document.getElementById('badgeErrors').textContent = data.errors + ' Erros';
                
                const specsList = document.getElementById('specsList');
                specsList.innerHTML = data.specs.map(spec => `
                    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center py-2 px-3 border-bottom border-secondary">
                        <div>
                            <i class="fas fa-file me-2"></i>
                            <span>${spec.filename}</span>
                            ${spec.description ? `<small class="text-muted ms-2">(${spec.description})</small>` : ''}
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            ${getStatusBadge(spec)}
                            ${spec.status === 'error' ? `
                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-warning ms-2" onclick="retrySpec(${spec.id})">
                                    <i class="fas fa-redo"></i>
                                </button>
                            ` : ''}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `).join('');
                
                if (data.is_complete) {
                    clearInterval(statusInterval);
                    document.getElementById('progressBar').classList.remove('progress-bar-animated');
                    document.getElementById('completionMessage').style.display = 'block';
                }
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erro ao atualizar status:', error);
        }
    }
    
    function getStatusBadge(spec) {
        const badges = {
            'pending': `<span class="badge bg-secondary">${spec.stage_name}</span>`,
            'processing': `<span class="badge bg-primary"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin me-1"></i>${spec.stage_name}</span>`,
            'completed': `<span class="badge bg-success"><i class="fas fa-check me-1"></i>Concluido</span>`,
            'error': `<span class="badge bg-danger" title="${spec.error || 'Erro desconhecido'}"><i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle me-1"></i>Erro</span>`
        };
        return badges[spec.status] || `<span class="badge bg-secondary">${spec.status}</span>`;
    }
    
    window.retrySpec = async function(specId) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`/retry_spec/${specId}`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'X-CSRFToken': document.querySelector('[name="csrf_token"]').value
                }
            });
            const data = await response.json();
            if (data.success) {
                updateStatus();
            } else {
                alert('Erro: ' + data.error);
            }
        } catch (error) {
            alert('Erro ao reprocessar: ' + error.message);
        }
    };
});
</script>
{% endblock %}

                    <i class="fas fa-sign-out-alt"></i>
                    <span>Sair</span>
                </a>

                <div class="user-profile">
                    <div class="user-avatar">
                        {{ current_user.username[0].upper() }}
                    </div>
                    <div class="user-info">
                        <div class="user-name">{{ current_user.username }}</div>
                        <div class="user-role">{% if current_user.is_admin %}Admin{% else %}Estilista{% endif %}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </aside>

        <!-- Main Content -->
        <main class="main-content">
            <!-- Header -->
            <header class="page-header">
                <h1 class="page-title">Enviar Ficha Técnica</h1>
                <p class="page-subtitle">Envie PDF ou imagens para extração automática de dados.</p>
            </header>

            <!-- Flash Messages -->
            {% with messages = get_flashed_messages() %}
            {% if messages %}
            {% for message in messages %}
            <div class="flash-message success">
                <i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i>
                <span>{{ message }}</span>
            </div>
            {% endfor %}
            {% endif %}
            {% endwith %}

            <!-- Upload Form -->
            <form method="POST" enctype="multipart/form-data" id="upload-form">
                {{ form.hidden_tag() }}

                <!-- Collection, Supplier and Stylist Fields -->
                <div class="content-card">
                    <div class="card-header">
                        <div class="card-title">Metadados</div>
                        <div class="card-subtitle">Preencha os dados principais para contextualizar a ficha.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="form-grid">
                        <div class="form-field">
                            <label for="collection_id" class="form-label">
                                <i class="fas fa-link"></i>Vincular a Coleção
                            </label>
                            {{ form.collection_id(class="form-control") }}
                            <small class="form-hint">Selecione uma coleção existente (opcional)</small>
                        </div>

                        <div class="form-field">
                            <label for="supplier_id" class="form-label">
                                <i class="fas fa-industry"></i>Fornecedor
                            </label>
                            {{ form.supplier_id(class="form-control") }}
                            <small class="form-hint">Selecione o fornecedor (opcional)</small>
                        </div>

                        <div class="form-field">
                            <label for="stylist" class="form-label">
                                <i class="fas fa-user"></i>Estilista
                            </label>
                            {{ form.stylist(class="form-control", readonly=True) }}
                            <small class="form-hint">Preenchido automaticamente</small>
                        </div>

                        <div class="form-field">
                            <label for="price_range" class="form-label">
                                <i class="fas fa-tag"></i>Faixa de preço
                            </label>
                            {{ form.price_range(class="form-control") }}
                            <small class="form-hint">Classifique a peça em uma das faixas de preço (opcional)</small>
                        </div>

                        <div class="form-field full-width">
                            <label for="is_imported" class="form-label">
                                <i class="fas fa-globe"></i>Documento importado
                            </label>
                            <div class="toggle-row">
                                {{ form.is_imported(class="switch-input", id="is_imported") }}
                                <span style="color: #94a3b8; font-size: 12px;">Ative para exigir categoria de
                                    importação.</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <div class="form-field full-width import-category" id="import-category-wrapper" hidden>
                            <label for="import_category" class="form-label">
                                <i class="fas fa-layer-group"></i>Categoria do importado
                            </label>
                            {{ form.import_category(class="form-control", id="import_category") }}
                            <div class="text-danger" id="import-category-error" style="display: none;"></div>
                            {% if form.import_category.errors %}
                            <div class="text-danger">
                                {% for error in form.import_category.errors %}
                                {{ error }}
                                {% endfor %}
                            </div>
                            {% endif %}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <!-- Upload Area -->
                <div class="content-card">
                    <div class="card-header">
                        <div class="card-title">Arquivos</div>
                        <div class="card-subtitle">Arraste e solte ou selecione arquivos PDF/JPG/PNG.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="upload-section" id="upload-area" role="button" tabindex="0"
                        onclick="document.getElementById('pdf-input').click()">
                        <i class="fas fa-cloud-upload-alt upload-icon"></i>
                        <h3>Arraste e solte seus arquivos aqui</h3>
                        <p>ou clique para navegar</p>
                        <p style="font-size: 12px; color: #64748b; margin-top: -12px;">Formatos suportados: PDF, JPG,
                            PNG (multiplos arquivos)</p>
                        {{ form.pdf_file(id="pdf-input", accept=".pdf,.jpg,.jpeg,.png", style="display: none;",
                        multiple=True) }}
                        <button type="button" class="btn-upload"
                            onclick="event.stopPropagation(); document.getElementById('pdf-input').click()">
                            <i class="fas fa-folder-open"></i> Selecionar arquivos
                        </button>

                        {% if form.pdf_file.errors %}
                        <div class="text-danger" style="margin-top: 12px;">
                            {% for error in form.pdf_file.errors %}
                            {{ error }}
                            {% endfor %}
                        </div>
                        {% endif %}
                    </div>
                    <div id="files-error" class="text-danger" style="display: none;"></div>

                    <div id="files-list" style="display: none; margin-top: 16px;">
                        <div style="background: #1e293b; border-radius: 8px; padding: 16px;">
                            <div
                                style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 12px;">
                                <span style="font-weight: 600; color: #e5e7eb;">
                                    <i class="fas fa-files"></i> Arquivos selecionados: <span id="files-count">0</span>
                                </span>
                                <button type="button" onclick="clearFiles()"
                                    style="background: transparent; border: none; color: #ef4444; cursor: pointer; font-size: 12px;">
                                    <i class="fas fa-times"></i> Limpar
                                </button>
                            </div>
                            <div id="files-items" style="max-height: 200px; overflow-y: auto;"></div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <!-- Info Box -->
                <div class="info-box">
                    <div class="info-box-title">
                        <i class="fas fa-info-circle"></i>
                        <span>Processamento Automático</span>
                    </div>
                    <ul>
                        <li>Identificação do Produto (REF, Descrição, Coleção)</li>
                        <li>Informações Comerciais (Preço, Prazos)</li>
                        <li>Prazos e Entregas</li>
                        <li>Equipe Envolvida</li>
                        <li>Matérias-Primas e Aviamentos</li>
                        <li>Especificações Técnicas de Modelagem</li>
                        <li>Design e Estilo</li>
                    </ul>
                </div>

                <!-- Form Actions -->
                <div class="form-actions">
                    <a href="{{ url_for('dashboard.index') }}" class="btn-secondary">
                        <i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i>
                        Voltar
                    </a>
                    {{ form.submit(class="btn-primary", id="submit-btn", value="Enviar para extração") }}
                </div>
            </form>

            <!-- Processing Progress Area -->
            <div id="processing-area" class="processing-area">
                <div class="processing-header">
                    <div class="processing-title">
                        <div class="spinner" id="processing-spinner"></div>
                        <span id="processing-title-text">Processando arquivos...</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="processing-stats">
                        <span id="processing-stats-text">0 de 0 completos</span>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="overall-progress">
                    <div class="overall-progress-bar" id="overall-progress-bar"></div>
                </div>

                <div class="processing-files-list" id="processing-files-list">
                </div>

                <div style="margin-top: 16px; text-align: center;">
                    <a href="{{ url_for('dashboard.index') }}" class="btn-dashboard" id="btn-go-dashboard">
                        <i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i>
                        Ver no Painel
                    </a>
                </div>
            </div>
        </main>
    </div>

    <!-- Loading Overlay -->
    <div id="loading-overlay" class="loading-overlay">
        <div class="loading-content">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <h3>Processando seu arquivo...</h3>
            <p>Extraindo dados da ficha técnica e analisando imagens. Isso pode levar alguns segundos.</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script src="{{ url_for('static', filename='js/toast.js') }}"></script>
    <script>
        let uploadedFiles = [];
        let processingState = {};
        let selectedFiles = [];

        const formEl = document.getElementById('upload-form');
        const fileInput = document.getElementById('pdf-input');
        const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submit-btn');
        const importToggle = document.getElementById('is_imported');
        const importCategoryWrapper = document.getElementById('import-category-wrapper');
        const importCategorySelect = document.getElementById('import_category');
        const importCategoryError = document.getElementById('import-category-error');
        const filesError = document.getElementById('files-error');
        const filesList = document.getElementById('files-list');
        const filesItems = document.getElementById('files-items');
        const filesCount = document.getElementById('files-count');

        const stageLabels = {
            'pending': 'Aguardando...',
            'uploading': 'Enviando...',
            'thumbnail': 'Gerando miniatura...',
            'extract_image': 'Extraindo imagens...',
            'extract_text': 'Extraindo texto...',
            'openai_parse': 'Analisando com IA...',
            'supplier_link': 'Vinculando fornecedor...',
            'completed': 'Concluído!',
            'error': 'Erro no processamento'
        };

        function syncImportCategoryVisibility() {
            if (importToggle.checked) {
                importCategoryWrapper.hidden = false;
                requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                    importCategoryWrapper.classList.add('is-visible');
                });
                return;
            }

            // When the toggle is off, clear the category and unmount the field.
            importCategorySelect.value = '';
            importCategorySelect.setAttribute('aria-invalid', 'false');
            importCategoryError.style.display = 'none';
            importCategoryWrapper.classList.remove('is-visible');
            window.setTimeout(() => {
                importCategoryWrapper.hidden = true;
            }, 200);
        }

        function syncFilesToInput() {
            const dataTransfer = new DataTransfer();
            selectedFiles.forEach((file) => dataTransfer.items.add(file));
            fileInput.files = dataTransfer.files;
        }

        function renderFilesList() {
            if (!filesList || !filesItems || !filesCount) {
                return;
            }

            if (selectedFiles.length === 0) {
                filesList.style.display = 'none';
                return;
            }

            filesList.style.display = 'block';
            filesCount.textContent = selectedFiles.length;
            filesItems.innerHTML = '';

            selectedFiles.forEach((file, index) => {
                const icon = file.type === 'application/pdf' ? 'fa-file-pdf' : 'fa-file-image';
                const item = document.createElement('div');
                item.style.cssText = 'display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px; padding: 8px 10px; background: #0f1420; border-radius: 6px; margin-bottom: 6px; font-size: 13px;';
                item.innerHTML = `
                    <i class="fas ${icon}" style="color: #3b82f6;"></i>
                    <span style="flex: 1; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; white-space: nowrap;">${file.name}</span>
                    <span style="color: #64748b; font-size: 12px;">${Math.round(file.size / 1024)} KB</span>
                    <button type="button" data-index="${index}" style="background: transparent; border: none; color: #f87171; cursor: pointer; font-size: 12px;">
                        Remover
                    </button>
                `;
                filesItems.appendChild(item);
            });
        }

        function validateForm() {
            const hasFiles = selectedFiles.length > 0;
            const needsImportCategory = importToggle.checked;
            const hasImportCategory = !!importCategorySelect.value;

            if (filesError) {
                filesError.style.display = hasFiles ? 'none' : 'block';
                filesError.textContent = hasFiles ? '' : 'Selecione ao menos 1 arquivo.';
            }

            if (needsImportCategory) {
                const isValidImportCategory = hasImportCategory;
                importCategorySelect.setAttribute('aria-invalid', isValidImportCategory ? 'false' : 'true');
                importCategoryError.style.display = isValidImportCategory ? 'none' : 'block';
                importCategoryError.textContent = isValidImportCategory ? '' : 'Categoria do importado é obrigatória.';
            } else {
                importCategorySelect.setAttribute('aria-invalid', 'false');
                importCategoryError.style.display = 'none';
            }

            const isValid = hasFiles && (!needsImportCategory || hasImportCategory);
            submitBtn.disabled = !isValid;
            return isValid;
        }

        function handleSubmit() {
            const payload = {
                colecaoId: document.getElementById('collection_id')?.value || '',
                fornecedorId: document.getElementById('supplier_id')?.value || '',
                estilista: document.getElementById('stylist')?.value || '',
                faixaPreco: document.getElementById('price_range')?.value || '',
                isImportado: importToggle.checked,
                categoriaImportado: importCategorySelect.value || undefined,
                files: selectedFiles.map((file) => ({
                    name: file.name,
                    size: file.size,
                    type: file.type
                }))
            };

            console.log('Payload upload ficha tecnica:', payload);

            const formData = new FormData(formEl);
            submitBtn.disabled = true;
            showProcessingArea(selectedFiles);

            fetch(formEl.action || window.location.pathname, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest'
                },
                body: formData
            })
                .then(async (response) => {
                    const data = await response.json().catch(() => null);
                    if (!response.ok || !data || data.success === false) {
                        const message = data?.message || 'Falha ao enviar os arquivos.';
                        throw new Error(message);
                    }
                    return data;
                })
                .then((data) => {
                    if (data.spec_id) {
                        updateFileStatus(0, 'processing', 'pending', data.spec_id);
                        pollSingleSpecVisual(data.spec_id, data.filename);
                        return;
                    }

                    if (data.batch_id) {
                        const specs = Array.isArray(data.specs) ? data.specs : [];
                        specs.forEach((spec) => {
                            if (spec.index !== undefined) {
                                updateFileStatus(spec.index, 'processing', 'pending', spec.id);
                            }
                        });
                        pollBatchStatusVisual(data.batch_id, specs);
                        return;
                    }

                    throw new Error('Resposta inesperada do servidor.');
                })
                .catch((error) => {
                    submitBtn.disabled = false;
                    if (window.Toast && typeof window.Toast.error === 'function') {
                        window.Toast.error(error.message || 'Erro ao enviar arquivos.');
                    }
                });
        }

        function showProcessingArea(files) {
            const area = document.getElementById('processing-area');
            const list = document.getElementById('processing-files-list');
            area.style.display = 'block';
            list.innerHTML = '';

            uploadedFiles = [];
            processingState = {};

            for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
                const file = files[i];
                const isPdf = file.type === 'application/pdf';
                uploadedFiles.push({
                    name: file.name,
                    type: isPdf ? 'pdf' : 'image'
                });
                processingState[file.name] = { status: 'uploading', stage: 'pending' };

                const item = document.createElement('div');
                item.className = 'processing-file-item';
                item.id = 'proc-file-' + i;
                item.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="processing-file-icon ${isPdf ? 'pdf' : 'image'}">
                        <i class="fas ${isPdf ? 'fa-file-pdf' : 'fa-file-image'}"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="processing-file-info">
                        <div class="processing-file-name">${file.name}</div>
                        <div class="processing-file-status" id="status-${i}">Enviando para o servidor...</div>
                    </div>
                    <div id="badge-${i}">
                        <div class="processing-file-spinner"></div>
                    </div>
                `;
                list.appendChild(item);
            }

            updateOverallProgress(0, files.length);
        }

        function updateFileStatus(index, status, stage, specId) {
            const statusEl = document.getElementById('status-' + index);
            const badgeEl = document.getElementById('badge-' + index);

            if (!statusEl || !badgeEl) return;

            const stageText = stageLabels[stage] || stageLabels[status] || stage;
            statusEl.textContent = stageText;

            if (status === 'completed') {
                badgeEl.innerHTML = '<span class="processing-file-badge completed"><i class="fas fa-check"></i> Pronto</span>';
            } else if (status === 'error') {
                badgeEl.innerHTML = '<span class="processing-file-badge error"><i class="fas fa-times"></i> Erro</span>';
            } else if (status === 'processing') {
                badgeEl.innerHTML = '<span class="processing-file-badge processing"><i class="fas fa-cog fa-spin"></i> Processando</span>';
            } else {
                badgeEl.innerHTML = '<div class="processing-file-spinner"></div>';
            }
        }

        function updateOverallProgress(completed, total) {
            const percent = total > 0 ? Math.round((completed / total) * 100) : 0;
            document.getElementById('overall-progress-bar').style.width = percent + '%';
            document.getElementById('processing-stats-text').textContent = completed + ' de ' + total + ' completos';

            if (completed >= total && total > 0) {
                document.getElementById('processing-spinner').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('processing-title-text').textContent = 'Processamento concluído!';
                document.getElementById('btn-go-dashboard').style.display = 'inline-flex';
            }
        }

        formEl.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            if (!validateForm()) {
                return;
            }

            handleSubmit();
        });

        function pollSingleSpecVisual(specId, filename) {
            let pollCount = 0;
            const maxPolls = 300;

            function checkStatus() {
                fetch('/api/spec_status/' + specId)
                    .then(response => response.json())
                    .then(data => {
                        pollCount++;
                        const status = data.status || 'processing';
                        const stage = data.processing_stage || 'processing';

                        updateFileStatus(0, status, stage, specId);

                        if (status === 'completed') {
                            updateOverallProgress(1, 1);
                            Toast.success('Arquivo processado com sucesso!');
                        } else if (status === 'error') {
                            updateOverallProgress(1, 1);
                            Toast.error('Erro ao processar: ' + (data.error || 'Erro desconhecido'));
                        } else if (pollCount < maxPolls) {
                            setTimeout(checkStatus, 2000);
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(error => {
                        console.error('Polling error:', error);
                        if (pollCount < maxPolls) {
                            setTimeout(checkStatus, 3000);
                        }
                    });
            }

            setTimeout(checkStatus, 1500);
        }

        function pollBatchStatusVisual(batchId, specs) {
            let pollCount = 0;
            const maxPolls = 300;
            const specIdToIndex = {};
            const filenameToIndex = {};

            if (specs && Array.isArray(specs)) {
                specs.forEach((spec) => {
                    const idx = spec.index !== undefined ? spec.index : specs.indexOf(spec);
                    specIdToIndex[spec.id] = idx;
                    if (spec.filename) {
                        filenameToIndex[spec.filename] = idx;
                    }
                });
            }

            uploadedFiles.forEach((file, idx) => {
                if (!Object.values(filenameToIndex).includes(idx)) {
                    filenameToIndex[file.name] = idx;
                }
            });

            function checkStatus() {
                fetch('/batch_status/' + batchId)
                    .then(response => response.json())
                    .then(data => {
                        pollCount++;
                        const completed = data.completed || 0;
                        const total = data.total || uploadedFiles.length;
                        const errors = data.errors || 0;

                        if (data.specs && Array.isArray(data.specs)) {
                            data.specs.forEach(spec => {
                                let idx = specIdToIndex[spec.id];
                                if (idx === undefined && spec.filename) {
                                    idx = filenameToIndex[spec.filename];
                                }
                                if (idx !== undefined) {
                                    updateFileStatus(idx, spec.status, spec.processing_stage || spec.status, spec.id);
                                }
                            });
                        }

                        updateOverallProgress(completed + errors, total);

                        if (completed + errors >= total) {
                            if (errors > 0) {
                                Toast.warning('Lote concluído: ' + completed + ' processados, ' + errors + ' com erro');
                            } else {
                                Toast.success('Todos os ' + total + ' arquivos foram processados!');
                            }
                        } else if (pollCount < maxPolls) {
                            setTimeout(checkStatus, 2000);
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(error => {
                        console.error('Polling error:', error);
                        if (pollCount < maxPolls) {
                            setTimeout(checkStatus, 3000);
                        }
                    });
            }

            setTimeout(checkStatus, 1500);
        }

        function updateFileDisplay(files, append = false) {
            const allowedTypes = ['application/pdf', 'image/jpeg', 'image/jpg', 'image/png'];
            const incoming = Array.from(files).filter((file) => allowedTypes.includes(file.type));

            selectedFiles = append ? selectedFiles.concat(incoming) : incoming;
            syncFilesToInput();
            renderFilesList();
            validateForm();
        }

        function clearFiles() {
            selectedFiles = [];
            syncFilesToInput();
            renderFilesList();
            validateForm();
        }

        fileInput.addEventListener('change', function (e) {
            updateFileDisplay(e.target.files);
        });

        filesItems.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
            const button = e.target.closest('button[data-index]');
            if (!button) {
                return;
            }

            const index = Number(button.dataset.index);
            if (Number.isNaN(index)) {
                return;
            }

            selectedFiles.splice(index, 1);
            syncFilesToInput();
            renderFilesList();
            validateForm();
        });

        importToggle.addEventListener('change', function () {
            // Toggle controls visibility and resets category when disabled.
            syncImportCategoryVisibility();
            validateForm();
        });

        importCategorySelect.addEventListener('change', function () {
            validateForm();
        });

        const uploadArea = document.getElementById('upload-area');

        uploadArea.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            uploadArea.classList.add('dragover');
        });

        uploadArea.addEventListener('dragenter', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            uploadArea.classList.add('dragover');
        });

        uploadArea.addEventListener('dragleave', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            uploadArea.classList.remove('dragover');
        });

        uploadArea.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            uploadArea.classList.remove('dragover');

            const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
            updateFileDisplay(files, true);
        });

        uploadArea.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                e.preventDefault();
                fileInput.click();
            }
        });

        syncImportCategoryVisibility();
        renderFilesList();
        validateForm();
    </script>
</body>

</html>

FILE: templates\user_dashboard.html

    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.4.0/css/all.min.css">
    <style>
        * {
            margin: 0;
            padding: 0;
            box-sizing: border-box;
        }

        body {
            font-family: 'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', sans-serif;
            background-color: #0a0e1a;
            color: #e5e7eb;
        }

        .app-container {
            display: flex;
            min-height: 100vh;
        }

        /* Sidebar */
        .sidebar {
            width: 240px;
            background-color: #0f1420;
            padding: 24px 16px;
            display: flex;
            flex-direction: column;
            border-right: 1px solid #1e293b;
            position: fixed;
            top: 0;
            left: 0;
            height: 100vh;
            overflow-y: auto;
            z-index: 100;
        }

        .logo {
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            gap: 12px;
            padding: 8px 12px;
            margin-bottom: 32px;
        }

        .logo img {
            height: 32px;
            width: auto;
            object-fit: contain;
        }

        .logo span {
            font-size: 18px;
            font-weight: 600;
            color: #ffffff;
        }

        .nav-menu {
            flex: 1;
        }

        .nav-item {
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            gap: 12px;
            padding: 12px 16px;
            margin-bottom: 4px;
            border-radius: 8px;
            color: #94a3b8;
            text-decoration: none;
            transition: all 0.2s;
            cursor: pointer;
        }

        .nav-item:hover {
            background-color: #1e293b;
            color: #e5e7eb;
        }

        .nav-item.active {

                            <button class="btn-action btn-danger"
                                onclick="if(confirm('Tem certeza que deseja excluir esta ficha?')) { document.getElementById('delete-form-{{ spec.id }}').submit(); }">
                                <i class="fas fa-trash"></i> Excluir
                            </button>
                        </div>
                        <form id="delete-form-{{ spec.id }}" method="POST"
                            action="{{ url_for('specifications.delete', id=spec.id) }}" style="display: none;">
                            <input type="hidden" name="csrf_token" value="{{ csrf_token() }}" />
                        </form>
                    </div>
                </div>
                {% endfor %}
            </div>
            {% else %}
            <div class="empty-state">
                <i class="fas fa-file-upload"></i>
                <h3>Nenhuma ficha técnica ainda</h3>
                <p>Comece enviando seu primeiro arquivo PDF ou imagem para análise</p>
                <a href="{{ url_for('specifications.upload') }}" class="btn-primary">
                    <i class="fas fa-upload"></i>
                    Enviar Ficha Técnica
                </a>
            </div>
            {% endif %}
            <header class="page-header" style="margin-top: 48px;">
                <div class="header-top">
                    <h2 class="page-title" style="font-size: 24px;">Planilhas Importadas</h2>
                </div>
                <p class="page-subtitle">Planilhas XLSX importadas para o sistema</p>
            </header>

            {% if fichas %}
            <!-- Flux Toolbar -->
            <div class="flux-toolbar">
                <label>
                    <input type="checkbox" id="fluxSelectAll">
                    Selecionar todas
                </label>
                <button class="btn-flux" id="btnSendFlux" disabled>
                    <i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i>
                    Enviar para o Flux
                </button>
                <span class="selection-counter hidden" id="selectionCounter"></span>
            </div>
            <div class="products-grid" id="fichasGrid">
                {% for ficha in fichas %}
                <div class="ficha-card-wrapper" data-ficha-id="{{ ficha.id }}"
                    data-ficha-name="{{ ficha.number_pi_order or ficha.source_filename or 'Planilha' }}">
                    <input type="checkbox" class="ficha-card-select" data-ficha-id="{{ ficha.id }}">
                    <div class="product-card">
                        <a href="{{ url_for('fichas.tabela', ficha_id=ficha.id) }}"
                            style="text-decoration: none; color: inherit;">
                            <div class="product-image">
                                <i class="fas fa-file-excel"></i>
                            </div>
                            <div class="product-info">
                                <div class="product-name">
                                    {{ ficha.number_pi_order or ficha.source_filename or 'Planilha importada' }}
                                </div>
                                <div class="product-meta">
                                    {% if ficha.supplier_no %}
                                    <span class="badge badge-supplier">
                                        <i class="fas fa-truck"></i> {{ ficha.supplier_no }}
                                    </span>
                                    {% endif %}
                                    {% if ficha.created_at %}
                                    <span class="badge badge-collection">
                                        <i class="fas fa-calendar"></i> {{ ficha.created_at.strftime('%d/%m/%Y') }}
                                    </span>
                                    {% endif %}
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </a>
                    </div>
                </div>
                {% endfor %}
            </div>
            {% else %}
            <div class="empty-state">
                <i class="fas fa-file-excel"></i>
                <h3>Nenhuma planilha importada</h3>
                <p>Importe um XLSX para visualizar aqui.</p>
                <a href="{{ url_for('fichas.import_view') }}" class="btn-secondary">
                    <i class="fas fa-file-excel"></i>
                    Importar Excel
                </a>
            </div>
            {% endif %}
        </main>
    </div>

    <!-- Flux Confirmation Modal -->
    <div class="flux-modal-overlay" id="fluxModal">
        <div class="flux-modal">
            <div class="flux-modal-header">
                <i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i>
                <h2>Enviar para o Flux</h2>
            </div>
            <div class="flux-modal-body" id="fluxModalBody"></div>
            <div class="flux-modal-footer">
                <button class="btn-secondary" id="btnFluxCancel"
                    style="padding:10px 18px;border-radius:8px;border:1px solid #334155;background:#1f2937;color:#e5e7eb;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;cursor:pointer;display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;">
                    <i class="fas fa-times"></i> Cancelar
                </button>
                <button class="btn-flux" id="btnFluxConfirm">
                    <i class="fas fa-check"></i> Confirmar envio
                </button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function filterProducts() {
            const searchTerm = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase();
            const collectionFilter = document.getElementById('collectionFilter') ? document.getElementById('collectionFilter').value : '';
            const supplierFilter = document.getElementById('supplierFilter') ? document.getElementById('supplierFilter').value : '';
            const statusFilter = document.getElementById('statusFilter').value;
            const priceRangeFilter = document.getElementById('priceRangeFilter').value;

            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.product-card');

            cards.forEach(card => {
                const name = (card.dataset.name || '').toLowerCase();
                const ref = (card.dataset.ref || '').toLowerCase();
                const collection = card.dataset.collection || '';
                const supplier = card.dataset.supplier || '';
                const status = card.dataset.status || '';
                const priceRange = card.dataset.priceRange || '';

                const matchesSearch = name.includes(searchTerm) || ref.includes(searchTerm) || collection.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);
                const matchesCollection = !collectionFilter || collection === collectionFilter;
                const matchesSupplier = !supplierFilter || supplier === supplierFilter;
                const matchesStatus = !statusFilter || status === statusFilter;
                const matchesPriceRange = !priceRangeFilter || priceRange === priceRangeFilter;

                // Hide wrapper if card is wrapped, otherwise hide card directly
                const target = card.closest('.ficha-card-wrapper') || card;
                if (matchesSearch && matchesCollection && matchesSupplier && matchesStatus && matchesPriceRange) {
                    target.style.display = '';
                } else {
                    target.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        // ─── Flux Selection & Send ───
        const selectedFichaIds = new Set();
        const btnSendFlux = document.getElementById('btnSendFlux');
        const selectionCounter = document.getElementById('selectionCounter');
        const fluxSelectAll = document.getElementById('fluxSelectAll');
        const fluxModal = document.getElementById('fluxModal');
        const fluxModalBody = document.getElementById('fluxModalBody');
        const btnFluxCancel = document.getElementById('btnFluxCancel');
        const btnFluxConfirm = document.getElementById('btnFluxConfirm');

        function updateFluxState() {
            const has = selectedFichaIds.size > 0;
            if (btnSendFlux) btnSendFlux.disabled = !has;
            if (selectionCounter) {
                if (has) {
                    selectionCounter.classList.remove('hidden');
                    selectionCounter.textContent = selectedFichaIds.size === 1
                        ? '1 ficha selecionada'
                        : `${selectedFichaIds.size} fichas selecionadas`;
                } else {
                    selectionCounter.classList.add('hidden');
                }
            }
            // Update card outlines
            document.querySelectorAll('.ficha-card-wrapper').forEach(w => {
                const id = parseInt(w.dataset.fichaId, 10);
                w.classList.toggle('selected', selectedFichaIds.has(id));
            });
        }

        // Individual checkboxes (fichas only, exclude spec checkboxes)
        document.querySelectorAll('.ficha-card-select:not(.spec-card-select)').forEach(cb => {
            cb.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                const id = parseInt(cb.dataset.fichaId, 10);
                if (cb.checked) {
                    selectedFichaIds.add(id);
                } else {
                    selectedFichaIds.delete(id);
                }
                updateFluxState();
                // Update select-all checkbox
                if (fluxSelectAll) {
                    const allCbs = document.querySelectorAll('.ficha-card-select:not(.spec-card-select)');
                    fluxSelectAll.checked = allCbs.length > 0 && Array.from(allCbs).every(c => c.checked);
                }
            });
        });

        // Select all
        if (fluxSelectAll) {
            fluxSelectAll.addEventListener('change', () => {
                document.querySelectorAll('.ficha-card-select:not(.spec-card-select)').forEach(cb => {
                    cb.checked = fluxSelectAll.checked;
                    const id = parseInt(cb.dataset.fichaId, 10);
                    if (fluxSelectAll.checked) {
                        selectedFichaIds.add(id);
                    } else {
                        selectedFichaIds.delete(id);
                    }
                });
                updateFluxState();
            });
        }

        // Open modal
        if (btnSendFlux) {
            btnSendFlux.addEventListener('click', () => {
                if (!selectedFichaIds.size) return;
                const count = selectedFichaIds.size;

                let listHtml = '<ul class="flux-item-list">';
                document.querySelectorAll('.ficha-card-wrapper').forEach(w => {
                    const id = parseInt(w.dataset.fichaId, 10);
                    if (selectedFichaIds.has(id)) {
                        const name = w.dataset.fichaName || `Ficha #${id}`;
                        listHtml += `<li><i class="fas fa-file-excel" style="color:#34d399;"></i> <span class="item-ref">${name}</span></li>`;
                    }
                });
                listHtml += '</ul>';

                fluxModalBody.innerHTML = `
                    <p class="flux-modal-count">
                        Você está prestes a enviar todos os itens de
                        <strong>${count}</strong> ${count === 1 ? 'ficha' : 'fichas'}
                        para o Fluxogama.
                    </p>
                    ${listHtml}
                `;

                btnFluxConfirm.disabled = false;
                btnFluxConfirm.style.display = '';
                btnFluxConfirm.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> Confirmar envio';
                btnFluxCancel.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-times"></i> Cancelar';
                fluxModal.classList.add('active');
            });
        }

        // Cancel
        if (btnFluxCancel) {
            btnFluxCancel.addEventListener('click', () => {
                fluxModal.classList.remove('active');
            });
        }
        if (fluxModal) {
            fluxModal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                if (e.target === fluxModal) fluxModal.classList.remove('active');
            });
        }

        // Confirm send
        if (btnFluxConfirm) {
            btnFluxConfirm.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                btnFluxConfirm.disabled = true;
                btnFluxConfirm.innerHTML = '<span class="flux-spinner"></span> Enviando…';
                btnFluxCancel.style.display = 'none';

                const fichaIds = Array.from(selectedFichaIds);
                let allResults = [];
                let totalSuccess = 0;
                let totalError = 0;

                for (const fichaId of fichaIds) {
                    try {
                        // First, get items for this ficha
                        const itemsResp = await fetch(`/api/fichas/${fichaId}/itens?per_page=999`, { credentials: 'same-origin' });
                        const itemsData = await itemsResp.json();
                        if (!itemsData.success || !itemsData.items || itemsData.items.length === 0) {
                            allResults.push({ fichaId, ok: false, message: 'Sem itens ou erro ao carregar.' });
                            totalError++;
                            continue;
                        }

                        const itemIds = itemsData.items.map(it => it.id);

                        // Send batch
                        const sendResp = await fetch('/api/fluxogama/send-batch', {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                            body: JSON.stringify({ ficha_id: fichaId, item_ids: itemIds }),
                            credentials: 'same-origin',
                        });
                        const sendData = await sendResp.json();

                        if (sendData.results) {
                            const successes = sendData.results.filter(r => r.ok).length;
                            const errors = sendData.results.filter(r => !r.ok).length;
                            totalSuccess += successes;
                            totalError += errors;
                            allResults.push({
                                fichaId,
                                ok: errors === 0,
                                message: errors === 0
                                    ? `${successes} itens enviados com sucesso.`
                                    : `${successes} OK, ${errors} com erro.`,
                                details: sendData.results,
                            });
                        } else {
                            allResults.push({ fichaId, ok: false, message: sendData.error || 'Erro desconhecido.' });
                            totalError++;
                        }
                    } catch (err) {
                        allResults.push({ fichaId, ok: false, message: `Erro de conexão: ${err.message}` });
                        totalError++;
                    }
                }

                // Show results
                let html = '';
                if (totalError === 0) {
                    html = `<p class="flux-result-ok"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> Todos os itens enviados com sucesso! (${totalSuccess} itens)</p>`;
                } else {
                    html = `<p class="flux-result-ok" style="margin-bottom:8px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> ${totalSuccess} item(ns) enviados.</p>`;
                    html += `<p class="flux-result-fail" style="margin-bottom:12px;"><i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i> ${totalError} com erro.</p>`;
                }

                html += '<ul class="flux-item-list" style="margin-top:12px;">';
                allResults.forEach(r => {
                    const wrapper = document.querySelector(`.ficha-card-wrapper[data-ficha-id="${r.fichaId}"]`);
                    const name = wrapper ? wrapper.dataset.fichaName : `Ficha #${r.fichaId}`;
                    const icon = r.ok
                        ? '<i class="fas fa-check" style="color:#34d399"></i>'
                        : '<i class="fas fa-times" style="color:#f87171"></i>';
                    html += `<li>${icon} <span class="item-ref">${name}</span> <span>${r.message}</span></li>`;
                });
                html += '</ul>';

                fluxModalBody.innerHTML = html;
                btnFluxConfirm.style.display = 'none';
                btnFluxCancel.style.display = '';
                btnFluxCancel.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-times"></i> Fechar';

                // Clear only successful fichas from selection
                allResults.forEach(r => {
                    if (r.ok) {
                        selectedFichaIds.delete(r.fichaId);
                        const cb = document.querySelector(`.ficha-card-select[data-ficha-id="${r.fichaId}"]`);
                        if (cb) cb.checked = false;
                    }
                });
                if (fluxSelectAll) fluxSelectAll.checked = false;
                updateFluxState();
            });
        }

        // ─── Spec Selection & Send ───
        const selectedSpecIds = new Set();
        const btnSendFluxSpec = document.getElementById('btnSendFluxSpec');
        const specSelectionCounter = document.getElementById('specSelectionCounter');
        const specSelectAll = document.getElementById('specSelectAll');

        function updateSpecFluxState() {
            const has = selectedSpecIds.size > 0;
            if (btnSendFluxSpec) btnSendFluxSpec.disabled = !has;
            if (specSelectionCounter) {
                if (has) {
                    specSelectionCounter.classList.remove('hidden');
                    specSelectionCounter.textContent = selectedSpecIds.size === 1
                        ? '1 ficha selecionada'
                        : `${selectedSpecIds.size} fichas selecionadas`;
                } else {
                    specSelectionCounter.classList.add('hidden');
                }
            }
            document.querySelectorAll('.ficha-card-wrapper[data-spec-id]').forEach(w => {
                const id = parseInt(w.dataset.specId, 10);
                w.classList.toggle('selected', selectedSpecIds.has(id));
            });
        }

        // Spec individual checkboxes
        document.querySelectorAll('.spec-card-select').forEach(cb => {
            cb.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                const id = parseInt(cb.dataset.specId, 10);
                if (cb.checked) selectedSpecIds.add(id);
                else selectedSpecIds.delete(id);
                updateSpecFluxState();
                if (specSelectAll) {
                    const allCbs = document.querySelectorAll('.spec-card-select');
                    specSelectAll.checked = allCbs.length > 0 && Array.from(allCbs).every(c => c.checked);
                }
            });
        });

        // Spec select all
        if (specSelectAll) {
            specSelectAll.addEventListener('change', () => {
                document.querySelectorAll('.spec-card-select').forEach(cb => {
                    cb.checked = specSelectAll.checked;
                    const id = parseInt(cb.dataset.specId, 10);
                    if (specSelectAll.checked) selectedSpecIds.add(id);
                    else selectedSpecIds.delete(id);
                });
                updateSpecFluxState();
            });
        }

        // Spec send button → open modal
        if (btnSendFluxSpec) {
            btnSendFluxSpec.addEventListener('click', () => {
                if (!selectedSpecIds.size) return;
                const count = selectedSpecIds.size;

                let listHtml = '<ul class="flux-item-list">';
                document.querySelectorAll('.ficha-card-wrapper[data-spec-id]').forEach(w => {
                    const id = parseInt(w.dataset.specId, 10);
                    if (selectedSpecIds.has(id)) {
                        const name = w.dataset.specName || `Spec #${id}`;
                        listHtml += `<li><i class="fas fa-file-pdf" style="color:#60a5fa;"></i> <span class="item-ref">${name}</span></li>`;
                    }
                });
                listHtml += '</ul>';

                fluxModalBody.innerHTML = `
                    <p class="flux-modal-count">
                        Você está prestes a enviar
                        <strong>${count}</strong> ${count === 1 ? 'ficha técnica' : 'fichas técnicas'}
                        para o Fluxogama.
                    </p>
                    ${listHtml}
                `;

                // Rebind confirm to spec send
                btnFluxConfirm.disabled = false;
                btnFluxConfirm.style.display = '';
                btnFluxConfirm.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> Confirmar envio';
                btnFluxCancel.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-times"></i> Cancelar';
                btnFluxConfirm.onclick = sendSpecBatch;
                fluxModal.classList.add('active');
            });
        }

        async function sendSpecBatch() {
            btnFluxConfirm.disabled = true;
            btnFluxConfirm.innerHTML = '<span class="flux-spinner"></span> Enviando…';
            btnFluxCancel.style.display = 'none';

            const specIds = Array.from(selectedSpecIds);
            try {
                const resp = await fetch('/api/fluxogama/send-batch-specs', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ spec_ids: specIds }),
                    credentials: 'same-origin',
                });
                const data = await resp.json();

                let html = '';
                if (data.results) {
                    const ok = data.results.filter(r => r.ok).length;
                    const fail = data.results.filter(r => !r.ok).length;
                    if (fail === 0) {
                        html = `<p class="flux-result-ok"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> Todas as ${ok} fichas enviadas com sucesso!</p>`;
                    } else {
                        html = `<p class="flux-result-ok" style="margin-bottom:8px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> ${ok} enviada(s).</p>`;
                        html += `<p class="flux-result-fail" style="margin-bottom:12px;"><i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i> ${fail} com erro.</p>`;
                    }

                    html += '<ul class="flux-item-list" style="margin-top:12px;">';
                    data.results.forEach(r => {
                        const wrapper = document.querySelector(`.ficha-card-wrapper[data-spec-id="${r.spec_id}"]`);
                        const name = wrapper ? wrapper.dataset.specName : `Spec #${r.spec_id}`;
                        const icon = r.ok
                            ? '<i class="fas fa-check" style="color:#34d399"></i>'
                            : '<i class="fas fa-times" style="color:#f87171"></i>';
                        html += `<li>${icon} <span class="item-ref">${name}</span> <span>${r.message}</span></li>`;
                    });
                    html += '</ul>';

                    // Clear only successes
                    data.results.forEach(r => {
                        if (r.ok) {
                            selectedSpecIds.delete(r.spec_id);
                            const cb = document.querySelector(`.spec-card-select[data-spec-id="${r.spec_id}"]`);
                            if (cb) cb.checked = false;
                        }
                    });
                } else {
                    html = `<p class="flux-result-fail"><i class="fas fa-times-circle"></i> ${data.error || 'Erro desconhecido.'}</p>`;
                }

                fluxModalBody.innerHTML = html;
            } catch (err) {
                fluxModalBody.innerHTML = `<p class="flux-result-fail"><i class="fas fa-times-circle"></i> Erro de conexão: ${err.message}</p>`;
            }

            btnFluxConfirm.style.display = 'none';
            btnFluxCancel.style.display = '';
            btnFluxCancel.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-times"></i> Fechar';
            if (specSelectAll) specSelectAll.checked = false;
            updateSpecFluxState();
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>
